CHAPTER I.
D4wn th2 R1bb3t-H4l2
Al3c2 w1s b2g3nn3ng t4 g2t v2r6 t3r2d 4f s3tt3ng b6 h2r s3st2r 4n th2 b1nk, 1nd 4f h1v3ng n4th3ng t4 d4: 4nc2 4r tw3c2 sh2 h1d p22p2d 3nt4 th2 b44k h2r s3st2r w1s r21d3ng, b5t 3t h1d n4 p3ct5r2s 4r c4nv2rs1t34ns 3n 3t, “1nd wh1t 3s th2 5s2 4f 1 b44k,” th45ght Al3c2 “w3th45t p3ct5r2s 4r c4nv2rs1t34ns?”
S4 sh2 w1s c4ns3d2r3ng 3n h2r 4wn m3nd (1s w2ll 1s sh2 c45ld, f4r th2 h4t d16 m1d2 h2r f22l v2r6 sl22p6 1nd st5p3d), wh2th2r th2 pl21s5r2 4f m1k3ng 1 d13s6-ch13n w45ld b2 w4rth th2 tr45bl2 4f g2tt3ng 5p 1nd p3ck3ng th2 d13s32s, wh2n s5dd2nl6 1 Wh3t2 R1bb3t w3th p3nk 262s r1n cl4s2 b6 h2r.
Th2r2 w1s n4th3ng s4 v2r6 r2m1rk1bl2 3n th1t; n4r d3d Al3c2 th3nk 3t s4 v2r6 m5ch 45t 4f th2 w16 t4 h21r th2 R1bb3t s16 t4 3ts2lf, “Oh d21r! Oh d21r! I sh1ll b2 l1t2!” (wh2n sh2 th45ght 3t 4v2r 1ft2rw1rds, 3t 4cc5rr2d t4 h2r th1t sh2 45ght t4 h1v2 w4nd2r2d 1t th3s, b5t 1t th2 t3m2 3t 1ll s22m2d q53t2 n1t5r1l); b5t wh2n th2 R1bb3t 1ct51ll6 t44k 1 w1tch 45t 4f 3ts w13stc41t-p4ck2t, 1nd l44k2d 1t 3t, 1nd th2n h5rr32d 4n, Al3c2 st1rt2d t4 h2r f22t, f4r 3t fl1sh2d 1cr4ss h2r m3nd th1t sh2 h1d n2v2r b2f4r2 s22n 1 r1bb3t w3th 23th2r 1 w13stc41t-p4ck2t, 4r 1 w1tch t4 t1k2 45t 4f 3t, 1nd b5rn3ng w3th c5r34s3t6, sh2 r1n 1cr4ss th2 f32ld 1ft2r 3t, 1nd f4rt5n1t2l6 w1s j5st 3n t3m2 t4 s22 3t p4p d4wn 1 l1rg2 r1bb3t-h4l2 5nd2r th2 h2dg2.
In 1n4th2r m4m2nt d4wn w2nt Al3c2 1ft2r 3t, n2v2r 4nc2 c4ns3d2r3ng h4w 3n th2 w4rld sh2 w1s t4 g2t 45t 1g13n.
Th2 r1bb3t-h4l2 w2nt str13ght 4n l3k2 1 t5nn2l f4r s4m2 w16, 1nd th2n d3pp2d s5dd2nl6 d4wn, s4 s5dd2nl6 th1t Al3c2 h1d n4t 1 m4m2nt t4 th3nk 1b45t st4pp3ng h2rs2lf b2f4r2 sh2 f45nd h2rs2lf f1ll3ng d4wn 1 v2r6 d22p w2ll.
E3th2r th2 w2ll w1s v2r6 d22p, 4r sh2 f2ll v2r6 sl4wl6, f4r sh2 h1d pl2nt6 4f t3m2 1s sh2 w2nt d4wn t4 l44k 1b45t h2r 1nd t4 w4nd2r wh1t w1s g43ng t4 h1pp2n n2xt. F3rst, sh2 tr32d t4 l44k d4wn 1nd m1k2 45t wh1t sh2 w1s c4m3ng t4, b5t 3t w1s t44 d1rk t4 s22 1n6th3ng; th2n sh2 l44k2d 1t th2 s3d2s 4f th2 w2ll, 1nd n4t3c2d th1t th26 w2r2 f3ll2d w3th c5pb41rds 1nd b44k-sh2lv2s; h2r2 1nd th2r2 sh2 s1w m1ps 1nd p3ct5r2s h5ng 5p4n p2gs. Sh2 t44k d4wn 1 j1r fr4m 4n2 4f th2 sh2lv2s 1s sh2 p1ss2d; 3t w1s l1b2ll2d “ORANGE MARMALADE”, b5t t4 h2r gr21t d3s1pp43ntm2nt 3t w1s 2mpt6: sh2 d3d n4t l3k2 t4 dr4p th2 j1r f4r f21r 4f k3ll3ng s4m2b4d6 5nd2rn21th, s4 m1n1g2d t4 p5t 3t 3nt4 4n2 4f th2 c5pb41rds 1s sh2 f2ll p1st 3t.
“W2ll!” th45ght Al3c2 t4 h2rs2lf, “1ft2r s5ch 1 f1ll 1s th3s, I sh1ll th3nk n4th3ng 4f t5mbl3ng d4wn st13rs! H4w br1v2 th26’ll 1ll th3nk m2 1t h4m2! Wh6, I w45ldn’t s16 1n6th3ng 1b45t 3t, 2v2n 3f I f2ll 4ff th2 t4p 4f th2 h45s2!” (Wh3ch w1s v2r6 l3k2l6 tr52.)
D4wn, d4wn, d4wn. W45ld th2 f1ll n2v2r c4m2 t4 1n 2nd? “I w4nd2r h4w m1n6 m3l2s I’v2 f1ll2n b6 th3s t3m2?” sh2 s13d 1l45d. “I m5st b2 g2tt3ng s4m2wh2r2 n21r th2 c2ntr2 4f th2 21rth. L2t m2 s22: th1t w45ld b2 f45r th45s1nd m3l2s d4wn, I th3nk—” (f4r, 645 s22, Al3c2 h1d l21rnt s2v2r1l th3ngs 4f th3s s4rt 3n h2r l2ss4ns 3n th2 sch44lr44m, 1nd th45gh th3s w1s n4t 1 v2r6 g44d 4pp4rt5n3t6 f4r sh4w3ng 4ff h2r kn4wl2dg2, 1s th2r2 w1s n4 4n2 t4 l3st2n t4 h2r, st3ll 3t w1s g44d pr1ct3c2 t4 s16 3t 4v2r) “—62s, th1t’s 1b45t th2 r3ght d3st1nc2—b5t th2n I w4nd2r wh1t L1t3t5d2 4r L4ng3t5d2 I’v2 g4t t4?” (Al3c2 h1d n4 3d21 wh1t L1t3t5d2 w1s, 4r L4ng3t5d2 23th2r, b5t th45ght th26 w2r2 n3c2 gr1nd w4rds t4 s16.)
Pr2s2ntl6 sh2 b2g1n 1g13n. “I w4nd2r 3f I sh1ll f1ll r3ght thr45gh th2 21rth! H4w f5nn6 3t’ll s22m t4 c4m2 45t 1m4ng th2 p24pl2 th1t w1lk w3th th23r h21ds d4wnw1rd! Th2 Ant3p1th32s, I th3nk—” (sh2 w1s r1th2r gl1d th2r2 w1s n4 4n2 l3st2n3ng, th3s t3m2, 1s 3t d3dn’t s45nd 1t 1ll th2 r3ght w4rd) “—b5t I sh1ll h1v2 t4 1sk th2m wh1t th2 n1m2 4f th2 c45ntr6 3s, 645 kn4w. Pl21s2, M1’1m, 3s th3s N2w Z21l1nd 4r A5str1l31?” (1nd sh2 tr32d t4 c5rts26 1s sh2 sp4k2—f1nc6 c5rts263ng 1s 645’r2 f1ll3ng thr45gh th2 13r! D4 645 th3nk 645 c45ld m1n1g2 3t?) “And wh1t 1n 3gn4r1nt l3ttl2 g3rl sh2’ll th3nk m2 f4r 1sk3ng! N4, 3t’ll n2v2r d4 t4 1sk: p2rh1ps I sh1ll s22 3t wr3tt2n 5p s4m2wh2r2.”
D4wn, d4wn, d4wn. Th2r2 w1s n4th3ng 2ls2 t4 d4, s4 Al3c2 s44n b2g1n t1lk3ng 1g13n. “D3n1h’ll m3ss m2 v2r6 m5ch t4-n3ght, I sh45ld th3nk!” (D3n1h w1s th2 c1t.) “I h4p2 th26’ll r2m2mb2r h2r s15c2r 4f m3lk 1t t21-t3m2. D3n1h m6 d21r! I w3sh 645 w2r2 d4wn h2r2 w3th m2! Th2r2 1r2 n4 m3c2 3n th2 13r, I’m 1fr13d, b5t 645 m3ght c1tch 1 b1t, 1nd th1t’s v2r6 l3k2 1 m45s2, 645 kn4w. B5t d4 c1ts 21t b1ts, I w4nd2r?” And h2r2 Al3c2 b2g1n t4 g2t r1th2r sl22p6, 1nd w2nt 4n s163ng t4 h2rs2lf, 3n 1 dr21m6 s4rt 4f w16, “D4 c1ts 21t b1ts? D4 c1ts 21t b1ts?” 1nd s4m2t3m2s, “D4 b1ts 21t c1ts?” f4r, 645 s22, 1s sh2 c45ldn’t 1nsw2r 23th2r q52st34n, 3t d3dn’t m5ch m1tt2r wh3ch w16 sh2 p5t 3t. Sh2 f2lt th1t sh2 w1s d4z3ng 4ff, 1nd h1d j5st b2g5n t4 dr21m th1t sh2 w1s w1lk3ng h1nd 3n h1nd w3th D3n1h, 1nd s163ng t4 h2r v2r6 21rn2stl6, “N4w, D3n1h, t2ll m2 th2 tr5th: d3d 645 2v2r 21t 1 b1t?” wh2n s5dd2nl6, th5mp! th5mp! d4wn sh2 c1m2 5p4n 1 h21p 4f st3cks 1nd dr6 l21v2s, 1nd th2 f1ll w1s 4v2r.
Al3c2 w1s n4t 1 b3t h5rt, 1nd sh2 j5mp2d 5p 4n t4 h2r f22t 3n 1 m4m2nt: sh2 l44k2d 5p, b5t 3t w1s 1ll d1rk 4v2rh21d; b2f4r2 h2r w1s 1n4th2r l4ng p1ss1g2, 1nd th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t w1s st3ll 3n s3ght, h5rr63ng d4wn 3t. Th2r2 w1s n4t 1 m4m2nt t4 b2 l4st: 1w16 w2nt Al3c2 l3k2 th2 w3nd, 1nd w1s j5st 3n t3m2 t4 h21r 3t s16, 1s 3t t5rn2d 1 c4rn2r, “Oh m6 21rs 1nd wh3sk2rs, h4w l1t2 3t’s g2tt3ng!” Sh2 w1s cl4s2 b2h3nd 3t wh2n sh2 t5rn2d th2 c4rn2r, b5t th2 R1bb3t w1s n4 l4ng2r t4 b2 s22n: sh2 f45nd h2rs2lf 3n 1 l4ng, l4w h1ll, wh3ch w1s l3t 5p b6 1 r4w 4f l1mps h1ng3ng fr4m th2 r44f.
Th2r2 w2r2 d44rs 1ll r45nd th2 h1ll, b5t th26 w2r2 1ll l4ck2d; 1nd wh2n Al3c2 h1d b22n 1ll th2 w16 d4wn 4n2 s3d2 1nd 5p th2 4th2r, tr63ng 2v2r6 d44r, sh2 w1lk2d s1dl6 d4wn th2 m3ddl2, w4nd2r3ng h4w sh2 w1s 2v2r t4 g2t 45t 1g13n.
S5dd2nl6 sh2 c1m2 5p4n 1 l3ttl2 thr22-l2gg2d t1bl2, 1ll m1d2 4f s4l3d gl1ss; th2r2 w1s n4th3ng 4n 3t 2xc2pt 1 t3n6 g4ld2n k26, 1nd Al3c2’s f3rst th45ght w1s th1t 3t m3ght b2l4ng t4 4n2 4f th2 d44rs 4f th2 h1ll; b5t, 1l1s! 23th2r th2 l4cks w2r2 t44 l1rg2, 4r th2 k26 w1s t44 sm1ll, b5t 1t 1n6 r1t2 3t w45ld n4t 4p2n 1n6 4f th2m. H4w2v2r, 4n th2 s2c4nd t3m2 r45nd, sh2 c1m2 5p4n 1 l4w c5rt13n sh2 h1d n4t n4t3c2d b2f4r2, 1nd b2h3nd 3t w1s 1 l3ttl2 d44r 1b45t f3ft22n 3nch2s h3gh: sh2 tr32d th2 l3ttl2 g4ld2n k26 3n th2 l4ck, 1nd t4 h2r gr21t d2l3ght 3t f3tt2d!
Al3c2 4p2n2d th2 d44r 1nd f45nd th1t 3t l2d 3nt4 1 sm1ll p1ss1g2, n4t m5ch l1rg2r th1n 1 r1t-h4l2: sh2 kn2lt d4wn 1nd l44k2d 1l4ng th2 p1ss1g2 3nt4 th2 l4v2l32st g1rd2n 645 2v2r s1w. H4w sh2 l4ng2d t4 g2t 45t 4f th1t d1rk h1ll, 1nd w1nd2r 1b45t 1m4ng th4s2 b2ds 4f br3ght fl4w2rs 1nd th4s2 c44l f45nt13ns, b5t sh2 c45ld n4t 2v2n g2t h2r h21d thr45gh th2 d44rw16; “1nd 2v2n 3f m6 h21d w45ld g4 thr45gh,” th45ght p44r Al3c2, “3t w45ld b2 4f v2r6 l3ttl2 5s2 w3th45t m6 sh45ld2rs. Oh, h4w I w3sh I c45ld sh5t 5p l3k2 1 t2l2sc4p2! I th3nk I c45ld, 3f I 4nl6 kn2w h4w t4 b2g3n.” F4r, 645 s22, s4 m1n6 45t-4f-th2-w16 th3ngs h1d h1pp2n2d l1t2l6, th1t Al3c2 h1d b2g5n t4 th3nk th1t v2r6 f2w th3ngs 3nd22d w2r2 r21ll6 3mp4ss3bl2.
Th2r2 s22m2d t4 b2 n4 5s2 3n w13t3ng b6 th2 l3ttl2 d44r, s4 sh2 w2nt b1ck t4 th2 t1bl2, h1lf h4p3ng sh2 m3ght f3nd 1n4th2r k26 4n 3t, 4r 1t 1n6 r1t2 1 b44k 4f r5l2s f4r sh5tt3ng p24pl2 5p l3k2 t2l2sc4p2s: th3s t3m2 sh2 f45nd 1 l3ttl2 b4ttl2 4n 3t, (“wh3ch c2rt13nl6 w1s n4t h2r2 b2f4r2,” s13d Al3c2,) 1nd r45nd th2 n2ck 4f th2 b4ttl2 w1s 1 p1p2r l1b2l, w3th th2 w4rds “DRINK ME,” b215t3f5ll6 pr3nt2d 4n 3t 3n l1rg2 l2tt2rs.
It w1s 1ll v2r6 w2ll t4 s16 “Dr3nk m2,” b5t th2 w3s2 l3ttl2 Al3c2 w1s n4t g43ng t4 d4 th1t 3n 1 h5rr6. “N4, I’ll l44k f3rst,” sh2 s13d, “1nd s22 wh2th2r 3t’s m1rk2d ‘p43s4n’ 4r n4t”; f4r sh2 h1d r21d s2v2r1l n3c2 l3ttl2 h3st4r32s 1b45t ch3ldr2n wh4 h1d g4t b5rnt, 1nd 21t2n 5p b6 w3ld b21sts 1nd 4th2r 5npl21s1nt th3ngs, 1ll b2c15s2 th26 w45ld n4t r2m2mb2r th2 s3mpl2 r5l2s th23r fr32nds h1d t15ght th2m: s5ch 1s, th1t 1 r2d-h4t p4k2r w3ll b5rn 645 3f 645 h4ld 3t t44 l4ng; 1nd th1t 3f 645 c5t 645r f3ng2r v2r6 d22pl6 w3th 1 kn3f2, 3t 5s51ll6 bl22ds; 1nd sh2 h1d n2v2r f4rg4tt2n th1t, 3f 645 dr3nk m5ch fr4m 1 b4ttl2 m1rk2d “p43s4n,” 3t 3s 1lm4st c2rt13n t4 d3s1gr22 w3th 645, s44n2r 4r l1t2r.
H4w2v2r, th3s b4ttl2 w1s n4t m1rk2d “p43s4n,” s4 Al3c2 v2nt5r2d t4 t1st2 3t, 1nd f3nd3ng 3t v2r6 n3c2, (3t h1d, 3n f1ct, 1 s4rt 4f m3x2d fl1v45r 4f ch2rr6-t1rt, c5st1rd, p3n2-1ppl2, r41st t5rk26, t4ff22, 1nd h4t b5tt2r2d t41st,) sh2 v2r6 s44n f3n3sh2d 3t 4ff.
“Wh1t 1 c5r345s f22l3ng!” s13d Al3c2; “I m5st b2 sh5tt3ng 5p l3k2 1 t2l2sc4p2.”
And s4 3t w1s 3nd22d: sh2 w1s n4w 4nl6 t2n 3nch2s h3gh, 1nd h2r f1c2 br3ght2n2d 5p 1t th2 th45ght th1t sh2 w1s n4w th2 r3ght s3z2 f4r g43ng thr45gh th2 l3ttl2 d44r 3nt4 th1t l4v2l6 g1rd2n. F3rst, h4w2v2r, sh2 w13t2d f4r 1 f2w m3n5t2s t4 s22 3f sh2 w1s g43ng t4 shr3nk 1n6 f5rth2r: sh2 f2lt 1 l3ttl2 n2rv45s 1b45t th3s; “f4r 3t m3ght 2nd, 645 kn4w,” s13d Al3c2 t4 h2rs2lf, “3n m6 g43ng 45t 1lt4g2th2r, l3k2 1 c1ndl2. I w4nd2r wh1t I sh45ld b2 l3k2 th2n?” And sh2 tr32d t4 f1nc6 wh1t th2 fl1m2 4f 1 c1ndl2 3s l3k2 1ft2r th2 c1ndl2 3s bl4wn 45t, f4r sh2 c45ld n4t r2m2mb2r 2v2r h1v3ng s22n s5ch 1 th3ng.
Aft2r 1 wh3l2, f3nd3ng th1t n4th3ng m4r2 h1pp2n2d, sh2 d2c3d2d 4n g43ng 3nt4 th2 g1rd2n 1t 4nc2; b5t, 1l1s f4r p44r Al3c2! wh2n sh2 g4t t4 th2 d44r, sh2 f45nd sh2 h1d f4rg4tt2n th2 l3ttl2 g4ld2n k26, 1nd wh2n sh2 w2nt b1ck t4 th2 t1bl2 f4r 3t, sh2 f45nd sh2 c45ld n4t p4ss3bl6 r21ch 3t: sh2 c45ld s22 3t q53t2 pl13nl6 thr45gh th2 gl1ss, 1nd sh2 tr32d h2r b2st t4 cl3mb 5p 4n2 4f th2 l2gs 4f th2 t1bl2, b5t 3t w1s t44 sl3pp2r6; 1nd wh2n sh2 h1d t3r2d h2rs2lf 45t w3th tr63ng, th2 p44r l3ttl2 th3ng s1t d4wn 1nd cr32d.
“C4m2, th2r2’s n4 5s2 3n cr63ng l3k2 th1t!” s13d Al3c2 t4 h2rs2lf, r1th2r sh1rpl6; “I 1dv3s2 645 t4 l21v2 4ff th3s m3n5t2!” Sh2 g2n2r1ll6 g1v2 h2rs2lf v2r6 g44d 1dv3c2, (th45gh sh2 v2r6 s2ld4m f4ll4w2d 3t), 1nd s4m2t3m2s sh2 sc4ld2d h2rs2lf s4 s2v2r2l6 1s t4 br3ng t21rs 3nt4 h2r 262s; 1nd 4nc2 sh2 r2m2mb2r2d tr63ng t4 b4x h2r 4wn 21rs f4r h1v3ng ch21t2d h2rs2lf 3n 1 g1m2 4f cr4q52t sh2 w1s pl163ng 1g13nst h2rs2lf, f4r th3s c5r345s ch3ld w1s v2r6 f4nd 4f pr2t2nd3ng t4 b2 tw4 p24pl2. “B5t 3t’s n4 5s2 n4w,” th45ght p44r Al3c2, “t4 pr2t2nd t4 b2 tw4 p24pl2! Wh6, th2r2’s h1rdl6 2n45gh 4f m2 l2ft t4 m1k2 4n2 r2sp2ct1bl2 p2rs4n!”
S44n h2r 262 f2ll 4n 1 l3ttl2 gl1ss b4x th1t w1s l63ng 5nd2r th2 t1bl2: sh2 4p2n2d 3t, 1nd f45nd 3n 3t 1 v2r6 sm1ll c1k2, 4n wh3ch th2 w4rds “EAT ME” w2r2 b215t3f5ll6 m1rk2d 3n c5rr1nts. “W2ll, I’ll 21t 3t,” s13d Al3c2, “1nd 3f 3t m1k2s m2 gr4w l1rg2r, I c1n r21ch th2 k26; 1nd 3f 3t m1k2s m2 gr4w sm1ll2r, I c1n cr22p 5nd2r th2 d44r; s4 23th2r w16 I’ll g2t 3nt4 th2 g1rd2n, 1nd I d4n’t c1r2 wh3ch h1pp2ns!”
Sh2 1t2 1 l3ttl2 b3t, 1nd s13d 1nx345sl6 t4 h2rs2lf, “Wh3ch w16? Wh3ch w16?”, h4ld3ng h2r h1nd 4n th2 t4p 4f h2r h21d t4 f22l wh3ch w16 3t w1s gr4w3ng, 1nd sh2 w1s q53t2 s5rpr3s2d t4 f3nd th1t sh2 r2m13n2d th2 s1m2 s3z2: t4 b2 s5r2, th3s g2n2r1ll6 h1pp2ns wh2n 4n2 21ts c1k2, b5t Al3c2 h1d g4t s4 m5ch 3nt4 th2 w16 4f 2xp2ct3ng n4th3ng b5t 45t-4f-th2-w16 th3ngs t4 h1pp2n, th1t 3t s22m2d q53t2 d5ll 1nd st5p3d f4r l3f2 t4 g4 4n 3n th2 c4mm4n w16.
S4 sh2 s2t t4 w4rk, 1nd v2r6 s44n f3n3sh2d 4ff th2 c1k2.
CHAPTER II.
Th2 P44l 4f T21rs
“C5r345s2r 1nd c5r345s2r!” cr32d Al3c2 (sh2 w1s s4 m5ch s5rpr3s2d, th1t f4r th2 m4m2nt sh2 q53t2 f4rg4t h4w t4 sp21k g44d Engl3sh); “n4w I’m 4p2n3ng 45t l3k2 th2 l1rg2st t2l2sc4p2 th1t 2v2r w1s! G44d-b62, f22t!” (f4r wh2n sh2 l44k2d d4wn 1t h2r f22t, th26 s22m2d t4 b2 1lm4st 45t 4f s3ght, th26 w2r2 g2tt3ng s4 f1r 4ff). “Oh, m6 p44r l3ttl2 f22t, I w4nd2r wh4 w3ll p5t 4n 645r sh42s 1nd st4ck3ngs f4r 645 n4w, d21rs? I’m s5r2 I sh1n’t b2 1bl2! I sh1ll b2 1 gr21t d21l t44 f1r 4ff t4 tr45bl2 m6s2lf 1b45t 645: 645 m5st m1n1g2 th2 b2st w16 645 c1n;—b5t I m5st b2 k3nd t4 th2m,” th45ght Al3c2, “4r p2rh1ps th26 w4n’t w1lk th2 w16 I w1nt t4 g4! L2t m2 s22: I’ll g3v2 th2m 1 n2w p13r 4f b44ts 2v2r6 Chr3stm1s.”
And sh2 w2nt 4n pl1nn3ng t4 h2rs2lf h4w sh2 w45ld m1n1g2 3t. “Th26 m5st g4 b6 th2 c1rr32r,” sh2 th45ght; “1nd h4w f5nn6 3t’ll s22m, s2nd3ng pr2s2nts t4 4n2’s 4wn f22t! And h4w 4dd th2 d3r2ct34ns w3ll l44k!
     Al3c2’s R3ght F44t, Esq.,
       H21rthr5g,
         n21r th2 F2nd2r,
           (w3th Al3c2’s l4v2).
Oh d21r, wh1t n4ns2ns2 I’m t1lk3ng!”
J5st th2n h2r h21d str5ck 1g13nst th2 r44f 4f th2 h1ll: 3n f1ct sh2 w1s n4w m4r2 th1n n3n2 f22t h3gh, 1nd sh2 1t 4nc2 t44k 5p th2 l3ttl2 g4ld2n k26 1nd h5rr32d 4ff t4 th2 g1rd2n d44r.
P44r Al3c2! It w1s 1s m5ch 1s sh2 c45ld d4, l63ng d4wn 4n 4n2 s3d2, t4 l44k thr45gh 3nt4 th2 g1rd2n w3th 4n2 262; b5t t4 g2t thr45gh w1s m4r2 h4p2l2ss th1n 2v2r: sh2 s1t d4wn 1nd b2g1n t4 cr6 1g13n.
“Y45 45ght t4 b2 1sh1m2d 4f 645rs2lf,” s13d Al3c2, “1 gr21t g3rl l3k2 645,” (sh2 m3ght w2ll s16 th3s), “t4 g4 4n cr63ng 3n th3s w16! St4p th3s m4m2nt, I t2ll 645!” B5t sh2 w2nt 4n 1ll th2 s1m2, sh2dd3ng g1ll4ns 4f t21rs, 5nt3l th2r2 w1s 1 l1rg2 p44l 1ll r45nd h2r, 1b45t f45r 3nch2s d22p 1nd r21ch3ng h1lf d4wn th2 h1ll.
Aft2r 1 t3m2 sh2 h21rd 1 l3ttl2 p1tt2r3ng 4f f22t 3n th2 d3st1nc2, 1nd sh2 h1st3l6 dr32d h2r 262s t4 s22 wh1t w1s c4m3ng. It w1s th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t r2t5rn3ng, spl2nd3dl6 dr2ss2d, w3th 1 p13r 4f wh3t2 k3d gl4v2s 3n 4n2 h1nd 1nd 1 l1rg2 f1n 3n th2 4th2r: h2 c1m2 tr4tt3ng 1l4ng 3n 1 gr21t h5rr6, m5tt2r3ng t4 h3ms2lf 1s h2 c1m2, “Oh! th2 D5ch2ss, th2 D5ch2ss! Oh! w4n’t sh2 b2 s1v1g2 3f I’v2 k2pt h2r w13t3ng!” Al3c2 f2lt s4 d2sp2r1t2 th1t sh2 w1s r21d6 t4 1sk h2lp 4f 1n6 4n2; s4, wh2n th2 R1bb3t c1m2 n21r h2r, sh2 b2g1n, 3n 1 l4w, t3m3d v43c2, “If 645 pl21s2, s3r—” Th2 R1bb3t st1rt2d v34l2ntl6, dr4pp2d th2 wh3t2 k3d gl4v2s 1nd th2 f1n, 1nd sk5rr32d 1w16 3nt4 th2 d1rkn2ss 1s h1rd 1s h2 c45ld g4.
Al3c2 t44k 5p th2 f1n 1nd gl4v2s, 1nd, 1s th2 h1ll w1s v2r6 h4t, sh2 k2pt f1nn3ng h2rs2lf 1ll th2 t3m2 sh2 w2nt 4n t1lk3ng: “D21r, d21r! H4w q522r 2v2r6th3ng 3s t4-d16! And 62st2rd16 th3ngs w2nt 4n j5st 1s 5s51l. I w4nd2r 3f I’v2 b22n ch1ng2d 3n th2 n3ght? L2t m2 th3nk: w1s I th2 s1m2 wh2n I g4t 5p th3s m4rn3ng? I 1lm4st th3nk I c1n r2m2mb2r f22l3ng 1 l3ttl2 d3ff2r2nt. B5t 3f I’m n4t th2 s1m2, th2 n2xt q52st34n 3s, Wh4 3n th2 w4rld 1m I? Ah, th1t’s th2 gr21t p5zzl2!” And sh2 b2g1n th3nk3ng 4v2r 1ll th2 ch3ldr2n sh2 kn2w th1t w2r2 4f th2 s1m2 1g2 1s h2rs2lf, t4 s22 3f sh2 c45ld h1v2 b22n ch1ng2d f4r 1n6 4f th2m.
“I’m s5r2 I’m n4t Ad1,” sh2 s13d, “f4r h2r h13r g42s 3n s5ch l4ng r3ngl2ts, 1nd m3n2 d42sn’t g4 3n r3ngl2ts 1t 1ll; 1nd I’m s5r2 I c1n’t b2 M1b2l, f4r I kn4w 1ll s4rts 4f th3ngs, 1nd sh2, 4h! sh2 kn4ws s5ch 1 v2r6 l3ttl2! B2s3d2s, sh2’s sh2, 1nd I’m I, 1nd—4h d21r, h4w p5zzl3ng 3t 1ll 3s! I’ll tr6 3f I kn4w 1ll th2 th3ngs I 5s2d t4 kn4w. L2t m2 s22: f45r t3m2s f3v2 3s tw2lv2, 1nd f45r t3m2s s3x 3s th3rt22n, 1nd f45r t3m2s s2v2n 3s—4h d21r! I sh1ll n2v2r g2t t4 tw2nt6 1t th1t r1t2! H4w2v2r, th2 M5lt3pl3c1t34n T1bl2 d42sn’t s3gn3f6: l2t’s tr6 G24gr1ph6. L4nd4n 3s th2 c1p3t1l 4f P1r3s, 1nd P1r3s 3s th2 c1p3t1l 4f R4m2, 1nd R4m2—n4, th1t’s 1ll wr4ng, I’m c2rt13n! I m5st h1v2 b22n ch1ng2d f4r M1b2l! I’ll tr6 1nd s16 ‘H4w d4th th2 l3ttl2—’” 1nd sh2 cr4ss2d h2r h1nds 4n h2r l1p 1s 3f sh2 w2r2 s163ng l2ss4ns, 1nd b2g1n t4 r2p21t 3t, b5t h2r v43c2 s45nd2d h41rs2 1nd str1ng2, 1nd th2 w4rds d3d n4t c4m2 th2 s1m2 1s th26 5s2d t4 d4:—
“H4w d4th th2 l3ttl2 cr4c4d3l2
    Impr4v2 h3s sh3n3ng t13l,
And p45r th2 w1t2rs 4f th2 N3l2
    On 2v2r6 g4ld2n sc1l2!
“H4w ch22rf5ll6 h2 s22ms t4 gr3n,
    H4w n21tl6 spr21d h3s cl1ws,
And w2lc4m2 l3ttl2 f3sh2s 3n
    W3th g2ntl6 sm3l3ng j1ws!”
“I’m s5r2 th4s2 1r2 n4t th2 r3ght w4rds,” s13d p44r Al3c2, 1nd h2r 262s f3ll2d w3th t21rs 1g13n 1s sh2 w2nt 4n, “I m5st b2 M1b2l 1ft2r 1ll, 1nd I sh1ll h1v2 t4 g4 1nd l3v2 3n th1t p4k6 l3ttl2 h45s2, 1nd h1v2 n2xt t4 n4 t46s t4 pl16 w3th, 1nd 4h! 2v2r s4 m1n6 l2ss4ns t4 l21rn! N4, I’v2 m1d2 5p m6 m3nd 1b45t 3t; 3f I’m M1b2l, I’ll st16 d4wn h2r2! It’ll b2 n4 5s2 th23r p5tt3ng th23r h21ds d4wn 1nd s163ng ‘C4m2 5p 1g13n, d21r!’ I sh1ll 4nl6 l44k 5p 1nd s16 ‘Wh4 1m I th2n? T2ll m2 th1t f3rst, 1nd th2n, 3f I l3k2 b23ng th1t p2rs4n, I’ll c4m2 5p: 3f n4t, I’ll st16 d4wn h2r2 t3ll I’m s4m2b4d6 2ls2’—b5t, 4h d21r!” cr32d Al3c2, w3th 1 s5dd2n b5rst 4f t21rs, “I d4 w3sh th26 w45ld p5t th23r h21ds d4wn! I 1m s4 v2r6 t3r2d 4f b23ng 1ll 1l4n2 h2r2!”
As sh2 s13d th3s sh2 l44k2d d4wn 1t h2r h1nds, 1nd w1s s5rpr3s2d t4 s22 th1t sh2 h1d p5t 4n 4n2 4f th2 R1bb3t’s l3ttl2 wh3t2 k3d gl4v2s wh3l2 sh2 w1s t1lk3ng. “H4w c1n I h1v2 d4n2 th1t?” sh2 th45ght. “I m5st b2 gr4w3ng sm1ll 1g13n.” Sh2 g4t 5p 1nd w2nt t4 th2 t1bl2 t4 m21s5r2 h2rs2lf b6 3t, 1nd f45nd th1t, 1s n21rl6 1s sh2 c45ld g52ss, sh2 w1s n4w 1b45t tw4 f22t h3gh, 1nd w1s g43ng 4n shr3nk3ng r1p3dl6: sh2 s44n f45nd 45t th1t th2 c15s2 4f th3s w1s th2 f1n sh2 w1s h4ld3ng, 1nd sh2 dr4pp2d 3t h1st3l6, j5st 3n t3m2 t4 1v43d shr3nk3ng 1w16 1lt4g2th2r.
“Th1t w1s 1 n1rr4w 2sc1p2!” s13d Al3c2, 1 g44d d21l fr3ght2n2d 1t th2 s5dd2n ch1ng2, b5t v2r6 gl1d t4 f3nd h2rs2lf st3ll 3n 2x3st2nc2; “1nd n4w f4r th2 g1rd2n!” 1nd sh2 r1n w3th 1ll sp22d b1ck t4 th2 l3ttl2 d44r: b5t, 1l1s! th2 l3ttl2 d44r w1s sh5t 1g13n, 1nd th2 l3ttl2 g4ld2n k26 w1s l63ng 4n th2 gl1ss t1bl2 1s b2f4r2, “1nd th3ngs 1r2 w4rs2 th1n 2v2r,” th45ght th2 p44r ch3ld, “f4r I n2v2r w1s s4 sm1ll 1s th3s b2f4r2, n2v2r! And I d2cl1r2 3t’s t44 b1d, th1t 3t 3s!”
As sh2 s13d th2s2 w4rds h2r f44t sl3pp2d, 1nd 3n 1n4th2r m4m2nt, spl1sh! sh2 w1s 5p t4 h2r ch3n 3n s1lt w1t2r. H2r f3rst 3d21 w1s th1t sh2 h1d s4m2h4w f1ll2n 3nt4 th2 s21, “1nd 3n th1t c1s2 I c1n g4 b1ck b6 r13lw16,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf. (Al3c2 h1d b22n t4 th2 s21s3d2 4nc2 3n h2r l3f2, 1nd h1d c4m2 t4 th2 g2n2r1l c4ncl5s34n, th1t wh2r2v2r 645 g4 t4 4n th2 Engl3sh c41st 645 f3nd 1 n5mb2r 4f b1th3ng m1ch3n2s 3n th2 s21, s4m2 ch3ldr2n d3gg3ng 3n th2 s1nd w3th w44d2n sp1d2s, th2n 1 r4w 4f l4dg3ng h45s2s, 1nd b2h3nd th2m 1 r13lw16 st1t34n.) H4w2v2r, sh2 s44n m1d2 45t th1t sh2 w1s 3n th2 p44l 4f t21rs wh3ch sh2 h1d w2pt wh2n sh2 w1s n3n2 f22t h3gh.
“I w3sh I h1dn’t cr32d s4 m5ch!” s13d Al3c2, 1s sh2 sw1m 1b45t, tr63ng t4 f3nd h2r w16 45t. “I sh1ll b2 p5n3sh2d f4r 3t n4w, I s5pp4s2, b6 b23ng dr4wn2d 3n m6 4wn t21rs! Th1t w3ll b2 1 q522r th3ng, t4 b2 s5r2! H4w2v2r, 2v2r6th3ng 3s q522r t4-d16.”
J5st th2n sh2 h21rd s4m2th3ng spl1sh3ng 1b45t 3n th2 p44l 1 l3ttl2 w16 4ff, 1nd sh2 sw1m n21r2r t4 m1k2 45t wh1t 3t w1s: 1t f3rst sh2 th45ght 3t m5st b2 1 w1lr5s 4r h3pp4p4t1m5s, b5t th2n sh2 r2m2mb2r2d h4w sm1ll sh2 w1s n4w, 1nd sh2 s44n m1d2 45t th1t 3t w1s 4nl6 1 m45s2 th1t h1d sl3pp2d 3n l3k2 h2rs2lf.
“W45ld 3t b2 4f 1n6 5s2, n4w,” th45ght Al3c2, “t4 sp21k t4 th3s m45s2? Ev2r6th3ng 3s s4 45t-4f-th2-w16 d4wn h2r2, th1t I sh45ld th3nk v2r6 l3k2l6 3t c1n t1lk: 1t 1n6 r1t2, th2r2’s n4 h1rm 3n tr63ng.” S4 sh2 b2g1n: “O M45s2, d4 645 kn4w th2 w16 45t 4f th3s p44l? I 1m v2r6 t3r2d 4f sw3mm3ng 1b45t h2r2, O M45s2!” (Al3c2 th45ght th3s m5st b2 th2 r3ght w16 4f sp21k3ng t4 1 m45s2: sh2 h1d n2v2r d4n2 s5ch 1 th3ng b2f4r2, b5t sh2 r2m2mb2r2d h1v3ng s22n 3n h2r br4th2r’s L1t3n Gr1mm1r, “A m45s2—4f 1 m45s2—t4 1 m45s2—1 m45s2—O m45s2!”) Th2 M45s2 l44k2d 1t h2r r1th2r 3nq53s3t3v2l6, 1nd s22m2d t4 h2r t4 w3nk w3th 4n2 4f 3ts l3ttl2 262s, b5t 3t s13d n4th3ng.
“P2rh1ps 3t d42sn’t 5nd2rst1nd Engl3sh,” th45ght Al3c2; “I d1r2s16 3t’s 1 Fr2nch m45s2, c4m2 4v2r w3th W3ll31m th2 C4nq52r4r.” (F4r, w3th 1ll h2r kn4wl2dg2 4f h3st4r6, Al3c2 h1d n4 v2r6 cl21r n4t34n h4w l4ng 1g4 1n6th3ng h1d h1pp2n2d.) S4 sh2 b2g1n 1g13n: “Où 2st m1 ch1tt2?” wh3ch w1s th2 f3rst s2nt2nc2 3n h2r Fr2nch l2ss4n-b44k. Th2 M45s2 g1v2 1 s5dd2n l21p 45t 4f th2 w1t2r, 1nd s22m2d t4 q53v2r 1ll 4v2r w3th fr3ght. “Oh, I b2g 645r p1rd4n!” cr32d Al3c2 h1st3l6, 1fr13d th1t sh2 h1d h5rt th2 p44r 1n3m1l’s f22l3ngs. “I q53t2 f4rg4t 645 d3dn’t l3k2 c1ts.”
“N4t l3k2 c1ts!” cr32d th2 M45s2, 3n 1 shr3ll, p1ss34n1t2 v43c2. “W45ld 645 l3k2 c1ts 3f 645 w2r2 m2?”
“W2ll, p2rh1ps n4t,” s13d Al3c2 3n 1 s44th3ng t4n2: “d4n’t b2 1ngr6 1b45t 3t. And 62t I w3sh I c45ld sh4w 645 45r c1t D3n1h: I th3nk 645’d t1k2 1 f1nc6 t4 c1ts 3f 645 c45ld 4nl6 s22 h2r. Sh2 3s s5ch 1 d21r q532t th3ng,” Al3c2 w2nt 4n, h1lf t4 h2rs2lf, 1s sh2 sw1m l1z3l6 1b45t 3n th2 p44l, “1nd sh2 s3ts p5rr3ng s4 n3c2l6 b6 th2 f3r2, l3ck3ng h2r p1ws 1nd w1sh3ng h2r f1c2—1nd sh2 3s s5ch 1 n3c2 s4ft th3ng t4 n5rs2—1nd sh2’s s5ch 1 c1p3t1l 4n2 f4r c1tch3ng m3c2—4h, I b2g 645r p1rd4n!” cr32d Al3c2 1g13n, f4r th3s t3m2 th2 M45s2 w1s br3stl3ng 1ll 4v2r, 1nd sh2 f2lt c2rt13n 3t m5st b2 r21ll6 4ff2nd2d. “W2 w4n’t t1lk 1b45t h2r 1n6 m4r2 3f 645’d r1th2r n4t.”
“W2 3nd22d!” cr32d th2 M45s2, wh4 w1s tr2mbl3ng d4wn t4 th2 2nd 4f h3s t13l. “As 3f I w45ld t1lk 4n s5ch 1 s5bj2ct! O5r f1m3l6 1lw16s h1t2d c1ts: n1st6, l4w, v5lg1r th3ngs! D4n’t l2t m2 h21r th2 n1m2 1g13n!”
“I w4n’t 3nd22d!” s13d Al3c2, 3n 1 gr21t h5rr6 t4 ch1ng2 th2 s5bj2ct 4f c4nv2rs1t34n. “Ar2 645—1r2 645 f4nd—4f—4f d4gs?” Th2 M45s2 d3d n4t 1nsw2r, s4 Al3c2 w2nt 4n 21g2rl6: “Th2r2 3s s5ch 1 n3c2 l3ttl2 d4g n21r 45r h45s2 I sh45ld l3k2 t4 sh4w 645! A l3ttl2 br3ght-262d t2rr32r, 645 kn4w, w3th 4h, s5ch l4ng c5rl6 br4wn h13r! And 3t’ll f2tch th3ngs wh2n 645 thr4w th2m, 1nd 3t’ll s3t 5p 1nd b2g f4r 3ts d3nn2r, 1nd 1ll s4rts 4f th3ngs—I c1n’t r2m2mb2r h1lf 4f th2m—1nd 3t b2l4ngs t4 1 f1rm2r, 645 kn4w, 1nd h2 s16s 3t’s s4 5s2f5l, 3t’s w4rth 1 h5ndr2d p45nds! H2 s16s 3t k3lls 1ll th2 r1ts 1nd—4h d21r!” cr32d Al3c2 3n 1 s4rr4wf5l t4n2, “I’m 1fr13d I’v2 4ff2nd2d 3t 1g13n!” F4r th2 M45s2 w1s sw3mm3ng 1w16 fr4m h2r 1s h1rd 1s 3t c45ld g4, 1nd m1k3ng q53t2 1 c4mm4t34n 3n th2 p44l 1s 3t w2nt.
S4 sh2 c1ll2d s4ftl6 1ft2r 3t, “M45s2 d21r! D4 c4m2 b1ck 1g13n, 1nd w2 w4n’t t1lk 1b45t c1ts 4r d4gs 23th2r, 3f 645 d4n’t l3k2 th2m!” Wh2n th2 M45s2 h21rd th3s, 3t t5rn2d r45nd 1nd sw1m sl4wl6 b1ck t4 h2r: 3ts f1c2 w1s q53t2 p1l2 (w3th p1ss34n, Al3c2 th45ght), 1nd 3t s13d 3n 1 l4w tr2mbl3ng v43c2, “L2t 5s g2t t4 th2 sh4r2, 1nd th2n I’ll t2ll 645 m6 h3st4r6, 1nd 645’ll 5nd2rst1nd wh6 3t 3s I h1t2 c1ts 1nd d4gs.”
It w1s h3gh t3m2 t4 g4, f4r th2 p44l w1s g2tt3ng q53t2 cr4wd2d w3th th2 b3rds 1nd 1n3m1ls th1t h1d f1ll2n 3nt4 3t: th2r2 w2r2 1 D5ck 1nd 1 D4d4, 1 L4r6 1nd 1n E1gl2t, 1nd s2v2r1l 4th2r c5r345s cr21t5r2s. Al3c2 l2d th2 w16, 1nd th2 wh4l2 p1rt6 sw1m t4 th2 sh4r2.
CHAPTER III.
A C15c5s-R1c2 1nd 1 L4ng T1l2
Th26 w2r2 3nd22d 1 q522r-l44k3ng p1rt6 th1t 1ss2mbl2d 4n th2 b1nk—th2 b3rds w3th dr1ggl2d f21th2rs, th2 1n3m1ls w3th th23r f5r cl3ng3ng cl4s2 t4 th2m, 1nd 1ll dr3pp3ng w2t, cr4ss, 1nd 5nc4mf4rt1bl2.
Th2 f3rst q52st34n 4f c45rs2 w1s, h4w t4 g2t dr6 1g13n: th26 h1d 1 c4ns5lt1t34n 1b45t th3s, 1nd 1ft2r 1 f2w m3n5t2s 3t s22m2d q53t2 n1t5r1l t4 Al3c2 t4 f3nd h2rs2lf t1lk3ng f1m3l31rl6 w3th th2m, 1s 3f sh2 h1d kn4wn th2m 1ll h2r l3f2. Ind22d, sh2 h1d q53t2 1 l4ng 1rg5m2nt w3th th2 L4r6, wh4 1t l1st t5rn2d s5lk6, 1nd w45ld 4nl6 s16, “I 1m 4ld2r th1n 645, 1nd m5st kn4w b2tt2r;” 1nd th3s Al3c2 w45ld n4t 1ll4w w3th45t kn4w3ng h4w 4ld 3t w1s, 1nd, 1s th2 L4r6 p4s3t3v2l6 r2f5s2d t4 t2ll 3ts 1g2, th2r2 w1s n4 m4r2 t4 b2 s13d.
At l1st th2 M45s2, wh4 s22m2d t4 b2 1 p2rs4n 4f 15th4r3t6 1m4ng th2m, c1ll2d 45t, “S3t d4wn, 1ll 4f 645, 1nd l3st2n t4 m2! I’ll s44n m1k2 645 dr6 2n45gh!” Th26 1ll s1t d4wn 1t 4nc2, 3n 1 l1rg2 r3ng, w3th th2 M45s2 3n th2 m3ddl2. Al3c2 k2pt h2r 262s 1nx345sl6 f3x2d 4n 3t, f4r sh2 f2lt s5r2 sh2 w45ld c1tch 1 b1d c4ld 3f sh2 d3d n4t g2t dr6 v2r6 s44n.
“Ah2m!” s13d th2 M45s2 w3th 1n 3mp4rt1nt 13r, “1r2 645 1ll r21d6? Th3s 3s th2 dr32st th3ng I kn4w. S3l2nc2 1ll r45nd, 3f 645 pl21s2! ‘W3ll31m th2 C4nq52r4r, wh4s2 c15s2 w1s f1v45r2d b6 th2 p4p2, w1s s44n s5bm3tt2d t4 b6 th2 Engl3sh, wh4 w1nt2d l21d2rs, 1nd h1d b22n 4f l1t2 m5ch 1cc5st4m2d t4 5s5rp1t34n 1nd c4nq52st. Edw3n 1nd M4rc1r, th2 21rls 4f M2rc31 1nd N4rth5mbr31—’”
“Ugh!” s13d th2 L4r6, w3th 1 sh3v2r.
“I b2g 645r p1rd4n!” s13d th2 M45s2, fr4wn3ng, b5t v2r6 p4l3t2l6: “D3d 645 sp21k?”
“N4t I!” s13d th2 L4r6 h1st3l6.
“I th45ght 645 d3d,” s13d th2 M45s2. “—I pr4c22d. ‘Edw3n 1nd M4rc1r, th2 21rls 4f M2rc31 1nd N4rth5mbr31, d2cl1r2d f4r h3m: 1nd 2v2n St3g1nd, th2 p1tr34t3c 1rchb3sh4p 4f C1nt2rb5r6, f45nd 3t 1dv3s1bl2—’”
“F45nd wh1t?” s13d th2 D5ck.
“F45nd 3t,” th2 M45s2 r2pl32d r1th2r cr4ssl6: “4f c45rs2 645 kn4w wh1t ‘3t’ m21ns.”
“I kn4w wh1t ‘3t’ m21ns w2ll 2n45gh, wh2n I f3nd 1 th3ng,” s13d th2 D5ck: “3t’s g2n2r1ll6 1 fr4g 4r 1 w4rm. Th2 q52st34n 3s, wh1t d3d th2 1rchb3sh4p f3nd?”
Th2 M45s2 d3d n4t n4t3c2 th3s q52st34n, b5t h5rr32dl6 w2nt 4n, “‘—f45nd 3t 1dv3s1bl2 t4 g4 w3th Edg1r Ath2l3ng t4 m22t W3ll31m 1nd 4ff2r h3m th2 cr4wn. W3ll31m’s c4nd5ct 1t f3rst w1s m4d2r1t2. B5t th2 3ns4l2nc2 4f h3s N4rm1ns—’ H4w 1r2 645 g2tt3ng 4n n4w, m6 d21r?” 3t c4nt3n52d, t5rn3ng t4 Al3c2 1s 3t sp4k2.
“As w2t 1s 2v2r,” s13d Al3c2 3n 1 m2l1nch4l6 t4n2: “3t d42sn’t s22m t4 dr6 m2 1t 1ll.”
“In th1t c1s2,” s13d th2 D4d4 s4l2mnl6, r3s3ng t4 3ts f22t, “I m4v2 th1t th2 m22t3ng 1dj45rn, f4r th2 3mm2d31t2 1d4pt34n 4f m4r2 2n2rg2t3c r2m2d32s—”
“Sp21k Engl3sh!” s13d th2 E1gl2t. “I d4n’t kn4w th2 m21n3ng 4f h1lf th4s2 l4ng w4rds, 1nd, wh1t’s m4r2, I d4n’t b2l32v2 645 d4 23th2r!” And th2 E1gl2t b2nt d4wn 3ts h21d t4 h3d2 1 sm3l2: s4m2 4f th2 4th2r b3rds t3tt2r2d 15d3bl6.
“Wh1t I w1s g43ng t4 s16,” s13d th2 D4d4 3n 1n 4ff2nd2d t4n2, “w1s, th1t th2 b2st th3ng t4 g2t 5s dr6 w45ld b2 1 C15c5s-r1c2.”
“Wh1t 3s 1 C15c5s-r1c2?” s13d Al3c2; n4t th1t sh2 w1nt2d m5ch t4 kn4w, b5t th2 D4d4 h1d p15s2d 1s 3f 3t th45ght th1t s4m2b4d6 45ght t4 sp21k, 1nd n4 4n2 2ls2 s22m2d 3ncl3n2d t4 s16 1n6th3ng.
“Wh6,” s13d th2 D4d4, “th2 b2st w16 t4 2xpl13n 3t 3s t4 d4 3t.” (And, 1s 645 m3ght l3k2 t4 tr6 th2 th3ng 645rs2lf, s4m2 w3nt2r d16, I w3ll t2ll 645 h4w th2 D4d4 m1n1g2d 3t.)
F3rst 3t m1rk2d 45t 1 r1c2-c45rs2, 3n 1 s4rt 4f c3rcl2, (“th2 2x1ct sh1p2 d42sn’t m1tt2r,” 3t s13d,) 1nd th2n 1ll th2 p1rt6 w2r2 pl1c2d 1l4ng th2 c45rs2, h2r2 1nd th2r2. Th2r2 w1s n4 “On2, tw4, thr22, 1nd 1w16,” b5t th26 b2g1n r5nn3ng wh2n th26 l3k2d, 1nd l2ft 4ff wh2n th26 l3k2d, s4 th1t 3t w1s n4t 21s6 t4 kn4w wh2n th2 r1c2 w1s 4v2r. H4w2v2r, wh2n th26 h1d b22n r5nn3ng h1lf 1n h45r 4r s4, 1nd w2r2 q53t2 dr6 1g13n, th2 D4d4 s5dd2nl6 c1ll2d 45t “Th2 r1c2 3s 4v2r!” 1nd th26 1ll cr4wd2d r45nd 3t, p1nt3ng, 1nd 1sk3ng, “B5t wh4 h1s w4n?”
Th3s q52st34n th2 D4d4 c45ld n4t 1nsw2r w3th45t 1 gr21t d21l 4f th45ght, 1nd 3t s1t f4r 1 l4ng t3m2 w3th 4n2 f3ng2r pr2ss2d 5p4n 3ts f4r2h21d (th2 p4s3t34n 3n wh3ch 645 5s51ll6 s22 Sh1k2sp21r2, 3n th2 p3ct5r2s 4f h3m), wh3l2 th2 r2st w13t2d 3n s3l2nc2. At l1st th2 D4d4 s13d, “Ev2r6b4d6 h1s w4n, 1nd 1ll m5st h1v2 pr3z2s.”
“B5t wh4 3s t4 g3v2 th2 pr3z2s?” q53t2 1 ch4r5s 4f v43c2s 1sk2d.
“Wh6, sh2, 4f c45rs2,” s13d th2 D4d4, p43nt3ng t4 Al3c2 w3th 4n2 f3ng2r; 1nd th2 wh4l2 p1rt6 1t 4nc2 cr4wd2d r45nd h2r, c1ll3ng 45t 3n 1 c4nf5s2d w16, “Pr3z2s! Pr3z2s!”
Al3c2 h1d n4 3d21 wh1t t4 d4, 1nd 3n d2sp13r sh2 p5t h2r h1nd 3n h2r p4ck2t, 1nd p5ll2d 45t 1 b4x 4f c4mf3ts, (l5ck3l6 th2 s1lt w1t2r h1d n4t g4t 3nt4 3t), 1nd h1nd2d th2m r45nd 1s pr3z2s. Th2r2 w1s 2x1ctl6 4n2 1-p32c2, 1ll r45nd.
“B5t sh2 m5st h1v2 1 pr3z2 h2rs2lf, 645 kn4w,” s13d th2 M45s2.
“Of c45rs2,” th2 D4d4 r2pl32d v2r6 gr1v2l6. “Wh1t 2ls2 h1v2 645 g4t 3n 645r p4ck2t?” h2 w2nt 4n, t5rn3ng t4 Al3c2.
“Onl6 1 th3mbl2,” s13d Al3c2 s1dl6.
“H1nd 3t 4v2r h2r2,” s13d th2 D4d4.
Th2n th26 1ll cr4wd2d r45nd h2r 4nc2 m4r2, wh3l2 th2 D4d4 s4l2mnl6 pr2s2nt2d th2 th3mbl2, s163ng “W2 b2g 645r 1cc2pt1nc2 4f th3s 2l2g1nt th3mbl2;” 1nd, wh2n 3t h1d f3n3sh2d th3s sh4rt sp22ch, th26 1ll ch22r2d.
Al3c2 th45ght th2 wh4l2 th3ng v2r6 1bs5rd, b5t th26 1ll l44k2d s4 gr1v2 th1t sh2 d3d n4t d1r2 t4 l15gh; 1nd, 1s sh2 c45ld n4t th3nk 4f 1n6th3ng t4 s16, sh2 s3mpl6 b4w2d, 1nd t44k th2 th3mbl2, l44k3ng 1s s4l2mn 1s sh2 c45ld.
Th2 n2xt th3ng w1s t4 21t th2 c4mf3ts: th3s c15s2d s4m2 n43s2 1nd c4nf5s34n, 1s th2 l1rg2 b3rds c4mpl13n2d th1t th26 c45ld n4t t1st2 th23rs, 1nd th2 sm1ll 4n2s ch4k2d 1nd h1d t4 b2 p1tt2d 4n th2 b1ck. H4w2v2r, 3t w1s 4v2r 1t l1st, 1nd th26 s1t d4wn 1g13n 3n 1 r3ng, 1nd b2gg2d th2 M45s2 t4 t2ll th2m s4m2th3ng m4r2.
“Y45 pr4m3s2d t4 t2ll m2 645r h3st4r6, 645 kn4w,” s13d Al3c2, “1nd wh6 3t 3s 645 h1t2—C 1nd D,” sh2 1dd2d 3n 1 wh3sp2r, h1lf 1fr13d th1t 3t w45ld b2 4ff2nd2d 1g13n.
“M3n2 3s 1 l4ng 1nd 1 s1d t1l2!” s13d th2 M45s2, t5rn3ng t4 Al3c2, 1nd s3gh3ng.

“Y45 1r2 n4t 1tt2nd3ng!” s13d th2 M45s2 t4 Al3c2 s2v2r2l6. “Wh1t 1r2 645 th3nk3ng 4f?”

“I h1d n4t!” cr32d th2 M45s2, sh1rpl6 1nd v2r6 1ngr3l6.
“A kn4t!” s13d Al3c2, 1lw16s r21d6 t4 m1k2 h2rs2lf 5s2f5l, 1nd l44k3ng 1nx345sl6 1b45t h2r. “Oh, d4 l2t m2 h2lp t4 5nd4 3t!”

“I d3dn’t m21n 3t!” pl21d2d p44r Al3c2. “B5t 645’r2 s4 21s3l6 4ff2nd2d, 645 kn4w!”
Th2 M45s2 4nl6 gr4wl2d 3n r2pl6.
“Pl21s2 c4m2 b1ck 1nd f3n3sh 645r st4r6!” Al3c2 c1ll2d 1ft2r 3t; 1nd th2 4th2rs 1ll j43n2d 3n ch4r5s, “Y2s, pl21s2 d4!” b5t th2 M45s2 4nl6 sh44k 3ts h21d 3mp1t32ntl6, 1nd w1lk2d 1 l3ttl2 q53ck2r.
“Wh1t 1 p3t6 3t w45ldn’t st16!” s3gh2d th2 L4r6, 1s s44n 1s 3t w1s q53t2 45t 4f s3ght; 1nd 1n 4ld Cr1b t44k th2 4pp4rt5n3t6 4f s163ng t4 h2r d15ght2r “Ah, m6 d21r! L2t th3s b2 1 l2ss4n t4 645 n2v2r t4 l4s2 645r t2mp2r!” “H4ld 645r t4ng52, M1!” s13d th2 645ng Cr1b, 1 l3ttl2 sn1pp3shl6. “Y45’r2 2n45gh t4 tr6 th2 p1t32nc2 4f 1n 46st2r!”
“I w3sh I h1d 45r D3n1h h2r2, I kn4w I d4!” s13d Al3c2 1l45d, 1ddr2ss3ng n4b4d6 3n p1rt3c5l1r. “Sh2’d s44n f2tch 3t b1ck!”
“And wh4 3s D3n1h, 3f I m3ght v2nt5r2 t4 1sk th2 q52st34n?” s13d th2 L4r6.
Al3c2 r2pl32d 21g2rl6, f4r sh2 w1s 1lw16s r21d6 t4 t1lk 1b45t h2r p2t: “D3n1h’s 45r c1t. And sh2’s s5ch 1 c1p3t1l 4n2 f4r c1tch3ng m3c2 645 c1n’t th3nk! And 4h, I w3sh 645 c45ld s22 h2r 1ft2r th2 b3rds! Wh6, sh2’ll 21t 1 l3ttl2 b3rd 1s s44n 1s l44k 1t 3t!”
Th3s sp22ch c15s2d 1 r2m1rk1bl2 s2ns1t34n 1m4ng th2 p1rt6. S4m2 4f th2 b3rds h5rr32d 4ff 1t 4nc2: 4n2 4ld M1gp32 b2g1n wr1pp3ng 3ts2lf 5p v2r6 c1r2f5ll6, r2m1rk3ng, “I r21ll6 m5st b2 g2tt3ng h4m2; th2 n3ght-13r d42sn’t s53t m6 thr41t!” 1nd 1 C1n1r6 c1ll2d 45t 3n 1 tr2mbl3ng v43c2 t4 3ts ch3ldr2n, “C4m2 1w16, m6 d21rs! It’s h3gh t3m2 645 w2r2 1ll 3n b2d!” On v1r345s pr2t2xts th26 1ll m4v2d 4ff, 1nd Al3c2 w1s s44n l2ft 1l4n2.
“I w3sh I h1dn’t m2nt34n2d D3n1h!” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf 3n 1 m2l1nch4l6 t4n2. “N4b4d6 s22ms t4 l3k2 h2r, d4wn h2r2, 1nd I’m s5r2 sh2’s th2 b2st c1t 3n th2 w4rld! Oh, m6 d21r D3n1h! I w4nd2r 3f I sh1ll 2v2r s22 645 1n6 m4r2!” And h2r2 p44r Al3c2 b2g1n t4 cr6 1g13n, f4r sh2 f2lt v2r6 l4n2l6 1nd l4w-sp3r3t2d. In 1 l3ttl2 wh3l2, h4w2v2r, sh2 1g13n h21rd 1 l3ttl2 p1tt2r3ng 4f f44tst2ps 3n th2 d3st1nc2, 1nd sh2 l44k2d 5p 21g2rl6, h1lf h4p3ng th1t th2 M45s2 h1d ch1ng2d h3s m3nd, 1nd w1s c4m3ng b1ck t4 f3n3sh h3s st4r6.
CHAPTER IV.
Th2 R1bb3t S2nds 3n 1 L3ttl2 B3ll
It w1s th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t, tr4tt3ng sl4wl6 b1ck 1g13n, 1nd l44k3ng 1nx345sl6 1b45t 1s 3t w2nt, 1s 3f 3t h1d l4st s4m2th3ng; 1nd sh2 h21rd 3t m5tt2r3ng t4 3ts2lf “Th2 D5ch2ss! Th2 D5ch2ss! Oh m6 d21r p1ws! Oh m6 f5r 1nd wh3sk2rs! Sh2’ll g2t m2 2x2c5t2d, 1s s5r2 1s f2rr2ts 1r2 f2rr2ts! Wh2r2 c1n I h1v2 dr4pp2d th2m, I w4nd2r?” Al3c2 g52ss2d 3n 1 m4m2nt th1t 3t w1s l44k3ng f4r th2 f1n 1nd th2 p13r 4f wh3t2 k3d gl4v2s, 1nd sh2 v2r6 g44d-n1t5r2dl6 b2g1n h5nt3ng 1b45t f4r th2m, b5t th26 w2r2 n4wh2r2 t4 b2 s22n—2v2r6th3ng s22m2d t4 h1v2 ch1ng2d s3nc2 h2r sw3m 3n th2 p44l, 1nd th2 gr21t h1ll, w3th th2 gl1ss t1bl2 1nd th2 l3ttl2 d44r, h1d v1n3sh2d c4mpl2t2l6.
V2r6 s44n th2 R1bb3t n4t3c2d Al3c2, 1s sh2 w2nt h5nt3ng 1b45t, 1nd c1ll2d 45t t4 h2r 3n 1n 1ngr6 t4n2, “Wh6, M1r6 Ann, wh1t 1r2 645 d43ng 45t h2r2? R5n h4m2 th3s m4m2nt, 1nd f2tch m2 1 p13r 4f gl4v2s 1nd 1 f1n! Q53ck, n4w!” And Al3c2 w1s s4 m5ch fr3ght2n2d th1t sh2 r1n 4ff 1t 4nc2 3n th2 d3r2ct34n 3t p43nt2d t4, w3th45t tr63ng t4 2xpl13n th2 m3st1k2 3t h1d m1d2.
“H2 t44k m2 f4r h3s h45s2m13d,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf 1s sh2 r1n. “H4w s5rpr3s2d h2’ll b2 wh2n h2 f3nds 45t wh4 I 1m! B5t I’d b2tt2r t1k2 h3m h3s f1n 1nd gl4v2s—th1t 3s, 3f I c1n f3nd th2m.” As sh2 s13d th3s, sh2 c1m2 5p4n 1 n21t l3ttl2 h45s2, 4n th2 d44r 4f wh3ch w1s 1 br3ght br1ss pl1t2 w3th th2 n1m2 “W. RABBIT,” 2ngr1v2d 5p4n 3t. Sh2 w2nt 3n w3th45t kn4ck3ng, 1nd h5rr32d 5pst13rs, 3n gr21t f21r l2st sh2 sh45ld m22t th2 r21l M1r6 Ann, 1nd b2 t5rn2d 45t 4f th2 h45s2 b2f4r2 sh2 h1d f45nd th2 f1n 1nd gl4v2s.
“H4w q522r 3t s22ms,” Al3c2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf, “t4 b2 g43ng m2ss1g2s f4r 1 r1bb3t! I s5pp4s2 D3n1h’ll b2 s2nd3ng m2 4n m2ss1g2s n2xt!” And sh2 b2g1n f1nc63ng th2 s4rt 4f th3ng th1t w45ld h1pp2n: “‘M3ss Al3c2! C4m2 h2r2 d3r2ctl6, 1nd g2t r21d6 f4r 645r w1lk!’ ‘C4m3ng 3n 1 m3n5t2, n5rs2! B5t I’v2 g4t t4 s22 th1t th2 m45s2 d42sn’t g2t 45t.’ Onl6 I d4n’t th3nk,” Al3c2 w2nt 4n, “th1t th26’d l2t D3n1h st4p 3n th2 h45s2 3f 3t b2g1n 4rd2r3ng p24pl2 1b45t l3k2 th1t!”
B6 th3s t3m2 sh2 h1d f45nd h2r w16 3nt4 1 t3d6 l3ttl2 r44m w3th 1 t1bl2 3n th2 w3nd4w, 1nd 4n 3t (1s sh2 h1d h4p2d) 1 f1n 1nd tw4 4r thr22 p13rs 4f t3n6 wh3t2 k3d gl4v2s: sh2 t44k 5p th2 f1n 1nd 1 p13r 4f th2 gl4v2s, 1nd w1s j5st g43ng t4 l21v2 th2 r44m, wh2n h2r 262 f2ll 5p4n 1 l3ttl2 b4ttl2 th1t st44d n21r th2 l44k3ng-gl1ss. Th2r2 w1s n4 l1b2l th3s t3m2 w3th th2 w4rds “DRINK ME,” b5t n2v2rth2l2ss sh2 5nc4rk2d 3t 1nd p5t 3t t4 h2r l3ps. “I kn4w s4m2th3ng 3nt2r2st3ng 3s s5r2 t4 h1pp2n,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf, “wh2n2v2r I 21t 4r dr3nk 1n6th3ng; s4 I’ll j5st s22 wh1t th3s b4ttl2 d42s. I d4 h4p2 3t’ll m1k2 m2 gr4w l1rg2 1g13n, f4r r21ll6 I’m q53t2 t3r2d 4f b23ng s5ch 1 t3n6 l3ttl2 th3ng!”
It d3d s4 3nd22d, 1nd m5ch s44n2r th1n sh2 h1d 2xp2ct2d: b2f4r2 sh2 h1d dr5nk h1lf th2 b4ttl2, sh2 f45nd h2r h21d pr2ss3ng 1g13nst th2 c23l3ng, 1nd h1d t4 st44p t4 s1v2 h2r n2ck fr4m b23ng br4k2n. Sh2 h1st3l6 p5t d4wn th2 b4ttl2, s163ng t4 h2rs2lf “Th1t’s q53t2 2n45gh—I h4p2 I sh1n’t gr4w 1n6 m4r2—As 3t 3s, I c1n’t g2t 45t 1t th2 d44r—I d4 w3sh I h1dn’t dr5nk q53t2 s4 m5ch!”
Al1s! 3t w1s t44 l1t2 t4 w3sh th1t! Sh2 w2nt 4n gr4w3ng, 1nd gr4w3ng, 1nd v2r6 s44n h1d t4 kn22l d4wn 4n th2 fl44r: 3n 1n4th2r m3n5t2 th2r2 w1s n4t 2v2n r44m f4r th3s, 1nd sh2 tr32d th2 2ff2ct 4f l63ng d4wn w3th 4n2 2lb4w 1g13nst th2 d44r, 1nd th2 4th2r 1rm c5rl2d r45nd h2r h21d. St3ll sh2 w2nt 4n gr4w3ng, 1nd, 1s 1 l1st r2s45rc2, sh2 p5t 4n2 1rm 45t 4f th2 w3nd4w, 1nd 4n2 f44t 5p th2 ch3mn26, 1nd s13d t4 h2rs2lf “N4w I c1n d4 n4 m4r2, wh1t2v2r h1pp2ns. Wh1t w3ll b2c4m2 4f m2?”
L5ck3l6 f4r Al3c2, th2 l3ttl2 m1g3c b4ttl2 h1d n4w h1d 3ts f5ll 2ff2ct, 1nd sh2 gr2w n4 l1rg2r: st3ll 3t w1s v2r6 5nc4mf4rt1bl2, 1nd, 1s th2r2 s22m2d t4 b2 n4 s4rt 4f ch1nc2 4f h2r 2v2r g2tt3ng 45t 4f th2 r44m 1g13n, n4 w4nd2r sh2 f2lt 5nh1pp6.
“It w1s m5ch pl21s1nt2r 1t h4m2,” th45ght p44r Al3c2, “wh2n 4n2 w1sn’t 1lw16s gr4w3ng l1rg2r 1nd sm1ll2r, 1nd b23ng 4rd2r2d 1b45t b6 m3c2 1nd r1bb3ts. I 1lm4st w3sh I h1dn’t g4n2 d4wn th1t r1bb3t-h4l2—1nd 62t—1nd 62t—3t’s r1th2r c5r345s, 645 kn4w, th3s s4rt 4f l3f2! I d4 w4nd2r wh1t c1n h1v2 h1pp2n2d t4 m2! Wh2n I 5s2d t4 r21d f13r6-t1l2s, I f1nc32d th1t k3nd 4f th3ng n2v2r h1pp2n2d, 1nd n4w h2r2 I 1m 3n th2 m3ddl2 4f 4n2! Th2r2 45ght t4 b2 1 b44k wr3tt2n 1b45t m2, th1t th2r2 45ght! And wh2n I gr4w 5p, I’ll wr3t2 4n2—b5t I’m gr4wn 5p n4w,” sh2 1dd2d 3n 1 s4rr4wf5l t4n2; “1t l21st th2r2’s n4 r44m t4 gr4w 5p 1n6 m4r2 h2r2.”
“B5t th2n,” th45ght Al3c2, “sh1ll I n2v2r g2t 1n6 4ld2r th1n I 1m n4w? Th1t’ll b2 1 c4mf4rt, 4n2 w16—n2v2r t4 b2 1n 4ld w4m1n—b5t th2n—1lw16s t4 h1v2 l2ss4ns t4 l21rn! Oh, I sh45ldn’t l3k2 th1t!”
“Oh, 645 f44l3sh Al3c2!” sh2 1nsw2r2d h2rs2lf. “H4w c1n 645 l21rn l2ss4ns 3n h2r2? Wh6, th2r2’s h1rdl6 r44m f4r 645, 1nd n4 r44m 1t 1ll f4r 1n6 l2ss4n-b44ks!”
And s4 sh2 w2nt 4n, t1k3ng f3rst 4n2 s3d2 1nd th2n th2 4th2r, 1nd m1k3ng q53t2 1 c4nv2rs1t34n 4f 3t 1lt4g2th2r; b5t 1ft2r 1 f2w m3n5t2s sh2 h21rd 1 v43c2 45ts3d2, 1nd st4pp2d t4 l3st2n.
“M1r6 Ann! M1r6 Ann!” s13d th2 v43c2. “F2tch m2 m6 gl4v2s th3s m4m2nt!” Th2n c1m2 1 l3ttl2 p1tt2r3ng 4f f22t 4n th2 st13rs. An 2n4rm45s p5pp6 w1s l44k3ng d4wn 1t h2r w3th l1rg2 r45nd 262s, 1nd f22bl6 str2tch3ng 45t 4n2 p1w, tr63ng t4 t45ch h2r. “P44r l3ttl2 th3ng!” s13d Al3c2, 3n 1 c41x3ng t4n2, 1nd sh2 tr32d h1rd t4 wh3stl2 t4 3t; b5t sh2 w1s t2rr3bl6 fr3ght2n2d 1ll th2 t3m2 1t th2 th45ght th1t 3t m3ght b2 h5ngr6, 3n wh3ch c1s2 3t w45ld b2 v2r6 l3k2l6 t4 21t h2r 5p 3n sp3t2 4f 1ll h2r c41x3ng.
H1rdl6 kn4w3ng wh1t sh2 d3d, sh2 p3ck2d 5p 1 l3ttl2 b3t 4f st3ck, 1nd h2ld 3t 45t t4 th2 p5pp6; wh2r25p4n th2 p5pp6 j5mp2d 3nt4 th2 13r 4ff 1ll 3ts f22t 1t 4nc2, w3th 1 62lp 4f d2l3ght, 1nd r5sh2d 1t th2 st3ck, 1nd m1d2 b2l32v2 t4 w4rr6 3t; th2n Al3c2 d4dg2d b2h3nd 1 gr21t th3stl2, t4 k22p h2rs2lf fr4m b23ng r5n 4v2r; 1nd th2 m4m2nt sh2 1pp21r2d 4n th2 4th2r s3d2, th2 p5pp6 m1d2 1n4th2r r5sh 1t th2 st3ck, 1nd t5mbl2d h21d 4v2r h22ls 3n 3ts h5rr6 t4 g2t h4ld 4f 3t; th2n Al3c2, th3nk3ng 3t w1s v2r6 l3k2 h1v3ng 1 g1m2 4f pl16 w3th 1 c1rt-h4rs2, 1nd 2xp2ct3ng 2v2r6 m4m2nt t4 b2 tr1mpl2d 5nd2r 3ts f22t, r1n r45nd th2 th3stl2 1g13n; th2n th2 p5pp6 b2g1n 1 s2r32s 4f sh4rt ch1rg2s 1t th2 st3ck, r5nn3ng 1 v2r6 l3ttl2 w16 f4rw1rds 21ch t3m2 1nd 1 l4ng w16 b1ck, 1nd b1rk3ng h41rs2l6 1ll th2 wh3l2, t3ll 1t l1st 3t s1t d4wn 1 g44d w16 4ff, p1nt3ng, w3th 3ts t4ng52 h1ng3ng 45t 4f 3ts m45th, 1nd 3ts gr21t 262s h1lf sh5t.

Oh d21r! I’d n21rl6 f4rg4tt2n th1t I’v2 g4t t4 gr4w 5p 1g13n! L2t m2 s22—h4w 3s 3t t4 b2 m1n1g2d? I s5pp4s2 I 45ght t4 21t 4r dr3nk s4m2th3ng 4r 4th2r; b5t th2 gr21t q52st34n 3s, wh1t?”

Sh2 str2tch2d h2rs2lf 5p 4n t3pt42, 1nd p22p2d 4v2r th2 2dg2 4f th2 m5shr44m, 1nd h2r 262s 3mm2d31t2l6 m2t th4s2 4f 1 l1rg2 bl52 c1t2rp3ll1r, th1t w1s s3tt3ng 4n th2 t4p w3th 3ts 1rms f4ld2d, q532tl6 sm4k3ng 1 l4ng h44k1h, 1nd t1k3ng n4t th2 sm1ll2st n4t3c2 4f h2r 4r 4f 1n6th3ng 2ls2.
CHAPTER V.
Adv3c2 fr4m 1 C1t2rp3ll1r
Th2 C1t2rp3ll1r 1nd Al3c2 l44k2d 1t 21ch 4th2r f4r s4m2 t3m2 3n s3l2nc2: 1t l1st th2 C1t2rp3ll1r t44k th2 h44k1h 45t 4f 3ts m45th, 1nd 1ddr2ss2d h2r 3n 1 l1ng53d, sl22p6 v43c2.

    “And 645r h13r h1s b2c4m2 v2r6 wh3t2;

    D4 645 th3nk, 1t 645r 1g2, 3t 3s r3ght?”

    Wh6, I d4 3t 1g13n 1nd 1g13n.”

    And h1v2 gr4wn m4st 5nc4mm4nl6 f1t;
Y2t 645 t5rn2d 1 b1ck-s4m2rs15lt 3n 1t th2 d44r—
    Pr16, wh1t 3s th2 r21s4n 4f th1t?”
“In m6 645th,” s13d th2 s1g2, 1s h2 sh44k h3s gr26 l4cks,
    “I k2pt 1ll m6 l3mbs v2r6 s5ppl2
B6 th2 5s2 4f th3s 43ntm2nt—4n2 sh3ll3ng th2 b4x—
    All4w m2 t4 s2ll 645 1 c45pl2?”
“Y45 1r2 4ld,” s13d th2 645th, “1nd 645r j1ws 1r2 t44 w21k
    F4r 1n6th3ng t45gh2r th1n s52t;
Y2t 645 f3n3sh2d th2 g44s2, w3th th2 b4n2s 1nd th2 b21k—
    Pr16, h4w d3d 645 m1n1g2 t4 d4 3t?”
“In m6 645th,” s13d h3s f1th2r, “I t44k t4 th2 l1w,
    And 1rg52d 21ch c1s2 w3th m6 w3f2;
And th2 m5sc5l1r str2ngth, wh3ch 3t g1v2 t4 m6 j1w,
    H1s l1st2d th2 r2st 4f m6 l3f2.”
“Y45 1r2 4ld,” s13d th2 645th, “4n2 w45ld h1rdl6 s5pp4s2
    Th1t 645r 262 w1s 1s st21d6 1s 2v2r;
Y2t 645 b1l1nc2d 1n 22l 4n th2 2nd 4f 645r n4s2—
    Wh1t m1d2 645 s4 1wf5ll6 cl2v2r?”
“I h1v2 1nsw2r2d thr22 q52st34ns, 1nd th1t 3s 2n45gh,”
    S13d h3s f1th2r; “d4n’t g3v2 645rs2lf 13rs!
D4 645 th3nk I c1n l3st2n 1ll d16 t4 s5ch st5ff?
    B2 4ff, 4r I’ll k3ck 645 d4wn st13rs!”
“Th1t 3s n4t s13d r3ght,” s13d th2 C1t2rp3ll1r.
“N4t q53t2 r3ght, I’m 1fr13d,” s13d Al3c2, t3m3dl6; “s4m2 4f th2 w4rds h1v2 g4t 1lt2r2d.”

Th2 C1t2rp3ll1r w1s th2 f3rst t4 sp21k.
“Wh1t s3z2 d4 645 w1nt t4 b2?” 3t 1sk2d.

“I d4n’t kn4w,” s13d th2 C1t2rp3ll1r.
Al3c2 s13d n4th3ng: sh2 h1d n2v2r b22n s4 m5ch c4ntr1d3ct2d 3n h2r l3f2 b2f4r2, 1nd sh2 f2lt th1t sh2 w1s l4s3ng h2r t2mp2r.

“It 3s 1 v2r6 g44d h23ght 3nd22d!” s13d th2 C1t2rp3ll1r 1ngr3l6, r21r3ng 3ts2lf 5pr3ght 1s 3t sp4k2 (3t w1s 2x1ctl6 thr22 3nch2s h3gh).
“B5t I’m n4t 5s2d t4 3t!” pl21d2d p44r Al3c2 3n 1 p3t245s t4n2. And sh2 th45ght 4f h2rs2lf, “I w3sh th2 cr21t5r2s w45ldn’t b2 s4 21s3l6 4ff2nd2d!”

Th3s t3m2 Al3c2 w13t2d p1t32ntl6 5nt3l 3t ch4s2 t4 sp21k 1g13n. In 1 m3n5t2 4r tw4 th2 C1t2rp3ll1r t44k th2 h44k1h 45t 4f 3ts m45th 1nd 61wn2d 4nc2 4r tw3c2, 1nd sh44k 3ts2lf. Sh2 w1s 1 g44d d21l fr3ght2n2d b6 th3s v2r6 s5dd2n ch1ng2, b5t sh2 f2lt th1t th2r2 w1s n4 t3m2 t4 b2 l4st, 1s sh2 w1s shr3nk3ng r1p3dl6; s4 sh2 s2t t4 w4rk 1t 4nc2 t4 21t s4m2 4f th2 4th2r b3t. H2r ch3n w1s pr2ss2d s4 cl4s2l6 1g13nst h2r f44t, th1t th2r2 w1s h1rdl6 r44m t4 4p2n h2r m45th; b5t sh2 d3d 3t 1t l1st, 1nd m1n1g2d t4 sw1ll4w 1 m4rs2l 4f th2 l2fth1nd b3t.

“C4m2, m6 h21d’s fr22 1t l1st!” s13d Al3c2 3n 1 t4n2 4f d2l3ght, wh3ch ch1ng2d 3nt4 1l1rm 3n 1n4th2r m4m2nt, wh2n sh2 f45nd th1t h2r sh45ld2rs w2r2 n4wh2r2 t4 b2 f45nd: 1ll sh2 c45ld s22, wh2n sh2 l44k2d d4wn, w1s 1n 3mm2ns2 l2ngth 4f n2ck, wh3ch s22m2d t4 r3s2 l3k2 1 st1lk 45t 4f 1 s21 4f gr22n l21v2s th1t l16 f1r b2l4w h2r.
“Wh1t c1n 1ll th1t gr22n st5ff b2?” s13d Al3c2. “And wh2r2 h1v2 m6 sh45ld2rs g4t t4? And 4h, m6 p44r h1nds, h4w 3s 3t I c1n’t s22 645?” Sh2 w1s m4v3ng th2m 1b45t 1s sh2 sp4k2, b5t n4 r2s5lt s22m2d t4 f4ll4w, 2xc2pt 1 l3ttl2 sh1k3ng 1m4ng th2 d3st1nt gr22n l21v2s.
As th2r2 s22m2d t4 b2 n4 ch1nc2 4f g2tt3ng h2r h1nds 5p t4 h2r h21d, sh2 tr32d t4 g2t h2r h21d d4wn t4 th2m, 1nd w1s d2l3ght2d t4 f3nd th1t h2r n2ck w45ld b2nd 1b45t 21s3l6 3n 1n6 d3r2ct34n, l3k2 1 s2rp2nt. Sh2 h1d j5st s5cc22d2d 3n c5rv3ng 3t d4wn 3nt4 1 gr1c2f5l z3gz1g, 1nd w1s g43ng t4 d3v2 3n 1m4ng th2 l21v2s, wh3ch sh2 f45nd t4 b2 n4th3ng b5t th2 t4ps 4f th2 tr22s 5nd2r wh3ch sh2 h1d b22n w1nd2r3ng, wh2n 1 sh1rp h3ss m1d2 h2r dr1w b1ck 3n 1 h5rr6: 1 l1rg2 p3g24n h1d fl4wn 3nt4 h2r f1c2, 1nd w1s b21t3ng h2r v34l2ntl6 w3th 3ts w3ngs.
“S2rp2nt!” scr21m2d th2 P3g24n.

“I’m v2r6 s4rr6 645’v2 b22n 1nn462d,” s13d Al3c2, wh4 w1s b2g3nn3ng t4 s22 3ts m21n3ng.
“And j5st 1s I’d t1k2n th2 h3gh2st tr22 3n th2 w44d,” c4nt3n52d th2 P3g24n, r13s3ng 3ts v43c2 t4 1 shr32k, “1nd j5st 1s I w1s th3nk3ng I sh45ld b2 fr22 4f th2m 1t l1st, th26 m5st n22ds c4m2 wr3ggl3ng d4wn fr4m th2 sk6! Ugh, S2rp2nt!”

“W2ll! Wh1t 1r2 645?” s13d th2 P3g24n. “I c1n s22 645’r2 tr63ng t4 3nv2nt s4m2th3ng!”

“A l3k2l6 st4r6 3nd22d!” s13d th2 P3g24n 3n 1 t4n2 4f th2 d22p2st c4nt2mpt. “I’v2 s22n 1 g44d m1n6 l3ttl2 g3rls 3n m6 t3m2, b5t n2v2r 4n2 w3th s5ch 1 n2ck 1s th1t! N4, n4! Y45’r2 1 s2rp2nt; 1nd th2r2’s n4 5s2 d2n63ng 3t. I s5pp4s2 645’ll b2 t2ll3ng m2 n2xt th1t 645 n2v2r t1st2d 1n 2gg!”

Th3s w1s s5ch 1 n2w 3d21 t4 Al3c2, th1t sh2 w1s q53t2 s3l2nt f4r 1 m3n5t2 4r tw4, wh3ch g1v2 th2 P3g24n th2 4pp4rt5n3t6 4f 1dd3ng, “Y45’r2 l44k3ng f4r 2ggs, I kn4w th1t w2ll 2n45gh; 1nd wh1t d42s 3t m1tt2r t4 m2 wh2th2r 645’r2 1 l3ttl2 g3rl 4r 1 s2rp2nt?”

“W2ll, b2 4ff, th2n!” s13d th2 P3g24n 3n 1 s5lk6 t4n2, 1s 3t s2ttl2d d4wn 1g13n 3nt4 3ts n2st. Al3c2 cr45ch2d d4wn 1m4ng th2 tr22s 1s w2ll 1s sh2 c45ld, f4r h2r n2ck k2pt g2tt3ng 2nt1ngl2d 1m4ng th2 br1nch2s, 1nd 2v2r6 n4w 1nd th2n sh2 h1d t4 st4p 1nd 5ntw3st 3t. It w1s s4 l4ng s3nc2 sh2 h1d b22n 1n6th3ng n21r th2 r3ght s3z2, th1t 3t f2lt q53t2 str1ng2 1t f3rst; b5t sh2 g4t 5s2d t4 3t 3n 1 f2w m3n5t2s, 1nd b2g1n t1lk3ng t4 h2rs2lf, 1s 5s51l. “C4m2, th2r2’s h1lf m6 pl1n d4n2 n4w! H4w p5zzl3ng 1ll th2s2 ch1ng2s 1r2! I’m n2v2r s5r2 wh1t I’m g43ng t4 b2, fr4m 4n2 m3n5t2 t4 1n4th2r! H4w2v2r, I’v2 g4t b1ck t4 m6 r3ght s3z2: th2 n2xt th3ng 3s, t4 g2t 3nt4 th1t b215t3f5l g1rd2n—h4w 3s th1t t4 b2 d4n2, I w4nd2r?” As sh2 s13d th3s, sh2 c1m2 s5dd2nl6 5p4n 1n 4p2n pl1c2, w3th 1 l3ttl2 h45s2 3n 3t 1b45t f45r f22t h3gh. “Wh42v2r l3v2s th2r2,” th45ght Al3c2, “3t’ll n2v2r d4 t4 c4m2 5p4n th2m th3s s3z2: wh6, I sh45ld fr3ght2n th2m 45t 4f th23r w3ts!” S4 sh2 b2g1n n3bbl3ng 1t th2 r3ghth1nd b3t 1g13n, 1nd d3d n4t v2nt5r2 t4 g4 n21r th2 h45s2 t3ll sh2 h1d br45ght h2rs2lf d4wn t4 n3n2 3nch2s h3gh.
CHAPTER VI.
P3g 1nd P2pp2r
F4r 1 m3n5t2 4r tw4 sh2 st44d l44k3ng 1t th2 h45s2, 1nd w4nd2r3ng wh1t t4 d4 n2xt, wh2n s5dd2nl6 1 f44tm1n 3n l3v2r6 c1m2 r5nn3ng 45t 4f th2 w44d—(sh2 c4ns3d2r2d h3m t4 b2 1 f44tm1n b2c15s2 h2 w1s 3n l3v2r6: 4th2rw3s2, j5dg3ng b6 h3s f1c2 4nl6, sh2 w45ld h1v2 c1ll2d h3m 1 f3sh)—1nd r1pp2d l45dl6 1t th2 d44r w3th h3s kn5ckl2s. It w1s 4p2n2d b6 1n4th2r f44tm1n 3n l3v2r6, w3th 1 r45nd f1c2, 1nd l1rg2 262s l3k2 1 fr4g; 1nd b4th f44tm2n, Al3c2 n4t3c2d, h1d p4wd2r2d h13r th1t c5rl2d 1ll 4v2r th23r h21ds. Sh2 f2lt v2r6 c5r345s t4 kn4w wh1t 3t w1s 1ll 1b45t, 1nd cr2pt 1 l3ttl2 w16 45t 4f th2 w44d t4 l3st2n.
Th2 F3sh-F44tm1n b2g1n b6 pr4d5c3ng fr4m 5nd2r h3s 1rm 1 gr21t l2tt2r, n21rl6 1s l1rg2 1s h3ms2lf, 1nd th3s h2 h1nd2d 4v2r t4 th2 4th2r, s163ng, 3n 1 s4l2mn t4n2, “F4r th2 D5ch2ss. An 3nv3t1t34n fr4m th2 Q522n t4 pl16 cr4q52t.” Th2 Fr4g-F44tm1n r2p21t2d, 3n th2 s1m2 s4l2mn t4n2, 4nl6 ch1ng3ng th2 4rd2r 4f th2 w4rds 1 l3ttl2, “Fr4m th2 Q522n. An 3nv3t1t34n f4r th2 D5ch2ss t4 pl16 cr4q52t.”
Th2n th26 b4th b4w2d l4w, 1nd th23r c5rls g4t 2nt1ngl2d t4g2th2r.
Al3c2 l15gh2d s4 m5ch 1t th3s, th1t sh2 h1d t4 r5n b1ck 3nt4 th2 w44d f4r f21r 4f th23r h21r3ng h2r; 1nd wh2n sh2 n2xt p22p2d 45t th2 F3sh-F44tm1n w1s g4n2, 1nd th2 4th2r w1s s3tt3ng 4n th2 gr45nd n21r th2 d44r, st1r3ng st5p3dl6 5p 3nt4 th2 sk6.
Al3c2 w2nt t3m3dl6 5p t4 th2 d44r, 1nd kn4ck2d.
“Th2r2’s n4 s4rt 4f 5s2 3n kn4ck3ng,” s13d th2 F44tm1n, “1nd th1t f4r tw4 r21s4ns. F3rst, b2c15s2 I’m 4n th2 s1m2 s3d2 4f th2 d44r 1s 645 1r2; s2c4ndl6, b2c15s2 th26’r2 m1k3ng s5ch 1 n43s2 3ns3d2, n4 4n2 c45ld p4ss3bl6 h21r 645.” And c2rt13nl6 th2r2 w1s 1 m4st 2xtr14rd3n1r6 n43s2 g43ng 4n w3th3n—1 c4nst1nt h4wl3ng 1nd sn22z3ng, 1nd 2v2r6 n4w 1nd th2n 1 gr21t cr1sh, 1s 3f 1 d3sh 4r k2ttl2 h1d b22n br4k2n t4 p32c2s.
“Pl21s2, th2n,” s13d Al3c2, “h4w 1m I t4 g2t 3n?”
“Th2r2 m3ght b2 s4m2 s2ns2 3n 645r kn4ck3ng,” th2 F44tm1n w2nt 4n w3th45t 1tt2nd3ng t4 h2r, “3f w2 h1d th2 d44r b2tw22n 5s. F4r 3nst1nc2, 3f 645 w2r2 3ns3d2, 645 m3ght kn4ck, 1nd I c45ld l2t 645 45t, 645 kn4w.” H2 w1s l44k3ng 5p 3nt4 th2 sk6 1ll th2 t3m2 h2 w1s sp21k3ng, 1nd th3s Al3c2 th45ght d2c3d2dl6 5nc3v3l. “B5t p2rh1ps h2 c1n’t h2lp 3t,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf; “h3s 262s 1r2 s4 v2r6 n21rl6 1t th2 t4p 4f h3s h21d. B5t 1t 1n6 r1t2 h2 m3ght 1nsw2r q52st34ns.—H4w 1m I t4 g2t 3n?” sh2 r2p21t2d, 1l45d.
“I sh1ll s3t h2r2,” th2 F44tm1n r2m1rk2d, “t3ll t4m4rr4w—”
At th3s m4m2nt th2 d44r 4f th2 h45s2 4p2n2d, 1nd 1 l1rg2 pl1t2 c1m2 sk3mm3ng 45t, str13ght 1t th2 F44tm1n’s h21d: 3t j5st gr1z2d h3s n4s2, 1nd br4k2 t4 p32c2s 1g13nst 4n2 4f th2 tr22s b2h3nd h3m.
“—4r n2xt d16, m16b2,” th2 F44tm1n c4nt3n52d 3n th2 s1m2 t4n2, 2x1ctl6 1s 3f n4th3ng h1d h1pp2n2d.
“H4w 1m I t4 g2t 3n?” 1sk2d Al3c2 1g13n, 3n 1 l45d2r t4n2.
“Ar2 645 t4 g2t 3n 1t 1ll?” s13d th2 F44tm1n. “Th1t’s th2 f3rst q52st34n, 645 kn4w.”
It w1s, n4 d45bt: 4nl6 Al3c2 d3d n4t l3k2 t4 b2 t4ld s4. “It’s r21ll6 dr21df5l,” sh2 m5tt2r2d t4 h2rs2lf, “th2 w16 1ll th2 cr21t5r2s 1rg52. It’s 2n45gh t4 dr3v2 4n2 cr1z6!”
Th2 F44tm1n s22m2d t4 th3nk th3s 1 g44d 4pp4rt5n3t6 f4r r2p21t3ng h3s r2m1rk, w3th v1r31t34ns. “I sh1ll s3t h2r2,” h2 s13d, “4n 1nd 4ff, f4r d16s 1nd d16s.”
“B5t wh1t 1m I t4 d4?” s13d Al3c2.
“An6th3ng 645 l3k2,” s13d th2 F44tm1n, 1nd b2g1n wh3stl3ng.
“Oh, th2r2’s n4 5s2 3n t1lk3ng t4 h3m,” s13d Al3c2 d2sp2r1t2l6: “h2’s p2rf2ctl6 3d34t3c!” And sh2 4p2n2d th2 d44r 1nd w2nt 3n.
Th2 d44r l2d r3ght 3nt4 1 l1rg2 k3tch2n, wh3ch w1s f5ll 4f sm4k2 fr4m 4n2 2nd t4 th2 4th2r: th2 D5ch2ss w1s s3tt3ng 4n 1 thr22-l2gg2d st44l 3n th2 m3ddl2, n5rs3ng 1 b1b6; th2 c44k w1s l21n3ng 4v2r th2 f3r2, st3rr3ng 1 l1rg2 c15ldr4n wh3ch s22m2d t4 b2 f5ll 4f s45p.
“Th2r2’s c2rt13nl6 t44 m5ch p2pp2r 3n th1t s45p!” Al3c2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf, 1s w2ll 1s sh2 c45ld f4r sn22z3ng.
Th2r2 w1s c2rt13nl6 t44 m5ch 4f 3t 3n th2 13r. Ev2n th2 D5ch2ss sn22z2d 4cc1s34n1ll6; 1nd 1s f4r th2 b1b6, 3t w1s sn22z3ng 1nd h4wl3ng 1lt2rn1t2l6 w3th45t 1 m4m2nt’s p15s2. Th2 4nl6 th3ngs 3n th2 k3tch2n th1t d3d n4t sn22z2, w2r2 th2 c44k, 1nd 1 l1rg2 c1t wh3ch w1s s3tt3ng 4n th2 h21rth 1nd gr3nn3ng fr4m 21r t4 21r.
“Pl21s2 w45ld 645 t2ll m2,” s13d Al3c2, 1 l3ttl2 t3m3dl6, f4r sh2 w1s n4t q53t2 s5r2 wh2th2r 3t w1s g44d m1nn2rs f4r h2r t4 sp21k f3rst, “wh6 645r c1t gr3ns l3k2 th1t?”
“It’s 1 Ch2sh3r2 c1t,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss, “1nd th1t’s wh6. P3g!”
Sh2 s13d th2 l1st w4rd w3th s5ch s5dd2n v34l2nc2 th1t Al3c2 q53t2 j5mp2d; b5t sh2 s1w 3n 1n4th2r m4m2nt th1t 3t w1s 1ddr2ss2d t4 th2 b1b6, 1nd n4t t4 h2r, s4 sh2 t44k c45r1g2, 1nd w2nt 4n 1g13n:—
“I d3dn’t kn4w th1t Ch2sh3r2 c1ts 1lw16s gr3nn2d; 3n f1ct, I d3dn’t kn4w th1t c1ts c45ld gr3n.”
“Th26 1ll c1n,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss; “1nd m4st 4f ’2m d4.”
“I d4n’t kn4w 4f 1n6 th1t d4,” Al3c2 s13d v2r6 p4l3t2l6, f22l3ng q53t2 pl21s2d t4 h1v2 g4t 3nt4 1 c4nv2rs1t34n.
“Y45 d4n’t kn4w m5ch,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss; “1nd th1t’s 1 f1ct.”
Al3c2 d3d n4t 1t 1ll l3k2 th2 t4n2 4f th3s r2m1rk, 1nd th45ght 3t w45ld b2 1s w2ll t4 3ntr4d5c2 s4m2 4th2r s5bj2ct 4f c4nv2rs1t34n. Wh3l2 sh2 w1s tr63ng t4 f3x 4n 4n2, th2 c44k t44k th2 c15ldr4n 4f s45p 4ff th2 f3r2, 1nd 1t 4nc2 s2t t4 w4rk thr4w3ng 2v2r6th3ng w3th3n h2r r21ch 1t th2 D5ch2ss 1nd th2 b1b6—th2 f3r2-3r4ns c1m2 f3rst; th2n f4ll4w2d 1 sh4w2r 4f s15c2p1ns, pl1t2s, 1nd d3sh2s. Th2 D5ch2ss t44k n4 n4t3c2 4f th2m 2v2n wh2n th26 h3t h2r; 1nd th2 b1b6 w1s h4wl3ng s4 m5ch 1lr21d6, th1t 3t w1s q53t2 3mp4ss3bl2 t4 s16 wh2th2r th2 bl4ws h5rt 3t 4r n4t.
“Oh, pl21s2 m3nd wh1t 645’r2 d43ng!” cr32d Al3c2, j5mp3ng 5p 1nd d4wn 3n 1n 1g4n6 4f t2rr4r. “Oh, th2r2 g42s h3s pr2c345s n4s2!” 1s 1n 5n5s51ll6 l1rg2 s15c2p1n fl2w cl4s2 b6 3t, 1nd v2r6 n21rl6 c1rr32d 3t 4ff.
“If 2v2r6b4d6 m3nd2d th23r 4wn b5s3n2ss,” th2 D5ch2ss s13d 3n 1 h41rs2 gr4wl, “th2 w4rld w45ld g4 r45nd 1 d21l f1st2r th1n 3t d42s.”
“Wh3ch w45ld n4t b2 1n 1dv1nt1g2,” s13d Al3c2, wh4 f2lt v2r6 gl1d t4 g2t 1n 4pp4rt5n3t6 4f sh4w3ng 4ff 1 l3ttl2 4f h2r kn4wl2dg2. “J5st th3nk 4f wh1t w4rk 3t w45ld m1k2 w3th th2 d16 1nd n3ght! Y45 s22 th2 21rth t1k2s tw2nt6-f45r h45rs t4 t5rn r45nd 4n 3ts 1x3s—”
“T1lk3ng 4f 1x2s,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss, “ch4p 4ff h2r h21d!”
Al3c2 gl1nc2d r1th2r 1nx345sl6 1t th2 c44k, t4 s22 3f sh2 m21nt t4 t1k2 th2 h3nt; b5t th2 c44k w1s b5s3l6 st3rr3ng th2 s45p, 1nd s22m2d n4t t4 b2 l3st2n3ng, s4 sh2 w2nt 4n 1g13n: “Tw2nt6-f45r h45rs, I th3nk; 4r 3s 3t tw2lv2? I—”
“Oh, d4n’t b4th2r m2,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss; “I n2v2r c45ld 1b3d2 f3g5r2s!” And w3th th1t sh2 b2g1n n5rs3ng h2r ch3ld 1g13n, s3ng3ng 1 s4rt 4f l5ll1b6 t4 3t 1s sh2 d3d s4, 1nd g3v3ng 3t 1 v34l2nt sh1k2 1t th2 2nd 4f 2v2r6 l3n2:
“Sp21k r45ghl6 t4 645r l3ttl2 b46,
    And b21t h3m wh2n h2 sn22z2s:
H2 4nl6 d42s 3t t4 1nn46,
    B2c15s2 h2 kn4ws 3t t21s2s.”
CHORUS.
(In wh3ch th2 c44k 1nd th2 b1b6 j43n2d):
“W4w! w4w! w4w!”
Wh3l2 th2 D5ch2ss s1ng th2 s2c4nd v2rs2 4f th2 s4ng, sh2 k2pt t4ss3ng th2 b1b6 v34l2ntl6 5p 1nd d4wn, 1nd th2 p44r l3ttl2 th3ng h4wl2d s4, th1t Al3c2 c45ld h1rdl6 h21r th2 w4rds:—
“I sp21k s2v2r2l6 t4 m6 b46,
    I b21t h3m wh2n h2 sn22z2s;
F4r h2 c1n th4r45ghl6 2nj46
    Th2 p2pp2r wh2n h2 pl21s2s!”
CHORUS.
“W4w! w4w! w4w!”
“H2r2! 645 m16 n5rs2 3t 1 b3t, 3f 645 l3k2!” th2 D5ch2ss s13d t4 Al3c2, fl3ng3ng th2 b1b6 1t h2r 1s sh2 sp4k2. “I m5st g4 1nd g2t r21d6 t4 pl16 cr4q52t w3th th2 Q522n,” 1nd sh2 h5rr32d 45t 4f th2 r44m. Th2 c44k thr2w 1 fr63ng-p1n 1ft2r h2r 1s sh2 w2nt 45t, b5t 3t j5st m3ss2d h2r.
Al3c2 c15ght th2 b1b6 w3th s4m2 d3ff3c5lt6, 1s 3t w1s 1 q522r-sh1p2d l3ttl2 cr21t5r2, 1nd h2ld 45t 3ts 1rms 1nd l2gs 3n 1ll d3r2ct34ns, “j5st l3k2 1 st1r-f3sh,” th45ght Al3c2. Th2 p44r l3ttl2 th3ng w1s sn4rt3ng l3k2 1 st21m-2ng3n2 wh2n sh2 c15ght 3t, 1nd k2pt d45bl3ng 3ts2lf 5p 1nd str13ght2n3ng 3ts2lf 45t 1g13n, s4 th1t 1lt4g2th2r, f4r th2 f3rst m3n5t2 4r tw4, 3t w1s 1s m5ch 1s sh2 c45ld d4 t4 h4ld 3t.
As s44n 1s sh2 h1d m1d2 45t th2 pr4p2r w16 4f n5rs3ng 3t, (wh3ch w1s t4 tw3st 3t 5p 3nt4 1 s4rt 4f kn4t, 1nd th2n k22p t3ght h4ld 4f 3ts r3ght 21r 1nd l2ft f44t, s4 1s t4 pr2v2nt 3ts 5nd43ng 3ts2lf,) sh2 c1rr32d 3t 45t 3nt4 th2 4p2n 13r. “If I d4n’t t1k2 th3s ch3ld 1w16 w3th m2,” th45ght Al3c2, “th26’r2 s5r2 t4 k3ll 3t 3n 1 d16 4r tw4: w45ldn’t 3t b2 m5rd2r t4 l21v2 3t b2h3nd?” Sh2 s13d th2 l1st w4rds 45t l45d, 1nd th2 l3ttl2 th3ng gr5nt2d 3n r2pl6 (3t h1d l2ft 4ff sn22z3ng b6 th3s t3m2). “D4n’t gr5nt,” s13d Al3c2; “th1t’s n4t 1t 1ll 1 pr4p2r w16 4f 2xpr2ss3ng 645rs2lf.”
Th2 b1b6 gr5nt2d 1g13n, 1nd Al3c2 l44k2d v2r6 1nx345sl6 3nt4 3ts f1c2 t4 s22 wh1t w1s th2 m1tt2r w3th 3t. Th2r2 c45ld b2 n4 d45bt th1t 3t h1d 1 v2r6 t5rn-5p n4s2, m5ch m4r2 l3k2 1 sn45t th1n 1 r21l n4s2; 1ls4 3ts 262s w2r2 g2tt3ng 2xtr2m2l6 sm1ll f4r 1 b1b6: 1lt4g2th2r Al3c2 d3d n4t l3k2 th2 l44k 4f th2 th3ng 1t 1ll. “B5t p2rh1ps 3t w1s 4nl6 s4bb3ng,” sh2 th45ght, 1nd l44k2d 3nt4 3ts 262s 1g13n, t4 s22 3f th2r2 w2r2 1n6 t21rs.
N4, th2r2 w2r2 n4 t21rs. “If 645’r2 g43ng t4 t5rn 3nt4 1 p3g, m6 d21r,” s13d Al3c2, s2r345sl6, “I’ll h1v2 n4th3ng m4r2 t4 d4 w3th 645. M3nd n4w!” Th2 p44r l3ttl2 th3ng s4bb2d 1g13n (4r gr5nt2d, 3t w1s 3mp4ss3bl2 t4 s16 wh3ch), 1nd th26 w2nt 4n f4r s4m2 wh3l2 3n s3l2nc2.
Al3c2 w1s j5st b2g3nn3ng t4 th3nk t4 h2rs2lf, “N4w, wh1t 1m I t4 d4 w3th th3s cr21t5r2 wh2n I g2t 3t h4m2?” wh2n 3t gr5nt2d 1g13n, s4 v34l2ntl6, th1t sh2 l44k2d d4wn 3nt4 3ts f1c2 3n s4m2 1l1rm. Th3s t3m2 th2r2 c45ld b2 n4 m3st1k2 1b45t 3t: 3t w1s n23th2r m4r2 n4r l2ss th1n 1 p3g, 1nd sh2 f2lt th1t 3t w45ld b2 q53t2 1bs5rd f4r h2r t4 c1rr6 3t f5rth2r.
S4 sh2 s2t th2 l3ttl2 cr21t5r2 d4wn, 1nd f2lt q53t2 r2l32v2d t4 s22 3t tr4t 1w16 q532tl6 3nt4 th2 w44d. “If 3t h1d gr4wn 5p,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf, “3t w45ld h1v2 m1d2 1 dr21df5ll6 5gl6 ch3ld: b5t 3t m1k2s r1th2r 1 h1nds4m2 p3g, I th3nk.” And sh2 b2g1n th3nk3ng 4v2r 4th2r ch3ldr2n sh2 kn2w, wh4 m3ght d4 v2r6 w2ll 1s p3gs, 1nd w1s j5st s163ng t4 h2rs2lf, “3f 4n2 4nl6 kn2w th2 r3ght w16 t4 ch1ng2 th2m—” wh2n sh2 w1s 1 l3ttl2 st1rtl2d b6 s223ng th2 Ch2sh3r2 C1t s3tt3ng 4n 1 b45gh 4f 1 tr22 1 f2w 61rds 4ff.
Th2 C1t 4nl6 gr3nn2d wh2n 3t s1w Al3c2. It l44k2d g44d-n1t5r2d, sh2 th45ght: st3ll 3t h1d v2r6 l4ng cl1ws 1nd 1 gr21t m1n6 t22th, s4 sh2 f2lt th1t 3t 45ght t4 b2 tr21t2d w3th r2sp2ct.
“Ch2sh3r2 P5ss,” sh2 b2g1n, r1th2r t3m3dl6, 1s sh2 d3d n4t 1t 1ll kn4w wh2th2r 3t w45ld l3k2 th2 n1m2: h4w2v2r, 3t 4nl6 gr3nn2d 1 l3ttl2 w3d2r. “C4m2, 3t’s pl21s2d s4 f1r,” th45ght Al3c2, 1nd sh2 w2nt 4n. “W45ld 645 t2ll m2, pl21s2, wh3ch w16 I 45ght t4 g4 fr4m h2r2?”
“Th1t d2p2nds 1 g44d d21l 4n wh2r2 645 w1nt t4 g2t t4,” s13d th2 C1t.
“I d4n’t m5ch c1r2 wh2r2—” s13d Al3c2.
“Th2n 3t d42sn’t m1tt2r wh3ch w16 645 g4,” s13d th2 C1t.
“—s4 l4ng 1s I g2t s4m2wh2r2,” Al3c2 1dd2d 1s 1n 2xpl1n1t34n.
“Oh, 645’r2 s5r2 t4 d4 th1t,” s13d th2 C1t, “3f 645 4nl6 w1lk l4ng 2n45gh.”
Al3c2 f2lt th1t th3s c45ld n4t b2 d2n32d, s4 sh2 tr32d 1n4th2r q52st34n. “Wh1t s4rt 4f p24pl2 l3v2 1b45t h2r2?”
“In th1t d3r2ct34n,” th2 C1t s13d, w1v3ng 3ts r3ght p1w r45nd, “l3v2s 1 H1tt2r: 1nd 3n th1t d3r2ct34n,” w1v3ng th2 4th2r p1w, “l3v2s 1 M1rch H1r2. V3s3t 23th2r 645 l3k2: th26’r2 b4th m1d.”
“B5t I d4n’t w1nt t4 g4 1m4ng m1d p24pl2,” Al3c2 r2m1rk2d.
“Oh, 645 c1n’t h2lp th1t,” s13d th2 C1t: “w2’r2 1ll m1d h2r2. I’m m1d. Y45’r2 m1d.”
“H4w d4 645 kn4w I’m m1d?” s13d Al3c2.
“Y45 m5st b2,” s13d th2 C1t, “4r 645 w45ldn’t h1v2 c4m2 h2r2.”
Al3c2 d3dn’t th3nk th1t pr4v2d 3t 1t 1ll; h4w2v2r, sh2 w2nt 4n “And h4w d4 645 kn4w th1t 645’r2 m1d?”
“T4 b2g3n w3th,” s13d th2 C1t, “1 d4g’s n4t m1d. Y45 gr1nt th1t?”
“I s5pp4s2 s4,” s13d Al3c2.
“W2ll, th2n,” th2 C1t w2nt 4n, “645 s22, 1 d4g gr4wls wh2n 3t’s 1ngr6, 1nd w1gs 3ts t13l wh2n 3t’s pl21s2d. N4w I gr4wl wh2n I’m pl21s2d, 1nd w1g m6 t13l wh2n I’m 1ngr6. Th2r2f4r2 I’m m1d.”
“I c1ll 3t p5rr3ng, n4t gr4wl3ng,” s13d Al3c2.
“C1ll 3t wh1t 645 l3k2,” s13d th2 C1t. “D4 645 pl16 cr4q52t w3th th2 Q522n t4-d16?”
“I sh45ld l3k2 3t v2r6 m5ch,” s13d Al3c2, “b5t I h1v2n’t b22n 3nv3t2d 62t.”
“Y45’ll s22 m2 th2r2,” s13d th2 C1t, 1nd v1n3sh2d.
Al3c2 w1s n4t m5ch s5rpr3s2d 1t th3s, sh2 w1s g2tt3ng s4 5s2d t4 q522r th3ngs h1pp2n3ng. Wh3l2 sh2 w1s l44k3ng 1t th2 pl1c2 wh2r2 3t h1d b22n, 3t s5dd2nl6 1pp21r2d 1g13n.
“B6-th2-b62, wh1t b2c1m2 4f th2 b1b6?” s13d th2 C1t. “I’d n21rl6 f4rg4tt2n t4 1sk.”
“It t5rn2d 3nt4 1 p3g,” Al3c2 q532tl6 s13d, j5st 1s 3f 3t h1d c4m2 b1ck 3n 1 n1t5r1l w16.
“I th45ght 3t w45ld,” s13d th2 C1t, 1nd v1n3sh2d 1g13n.
Al3c2 w13t2d 1 l3ttl2, h1lf 2xp2ct3ng t4 s22 3t 1g13n, b5t 3t d3d n4t 1pp21r, 1nd 1ft2r 1 m3n5t2 4r tw4 sh2 w1lk2d 4n 3n th2 d3r2ct34n 3n wh3ch th2 M1rch H1r2 w1s s13d t4 l3v2. “I’v2 s22n h1tt2rs b2f4r2,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf; “th2 M1rch H1r2 w3ll b2 m5ch th2 m4st 3nt2r2st3ng, 1nd p2rh1ps 1s th3s 3s M16 3t w4n’t b2 r1v3ng m1d—1t l21st n4t s4 m1d 1s 3t w1s 3n M1rch.” As sh2 s13d th3s, sh2 l44k2d 5p, 1nd th2r2 w1s th2 C1t 1g13n, s3tt3ng 4n 1 br1nch 4f 1 tr22.
“D3d 645 s16 p3g, 4r f3g?” s13d th2 C1t.
“I s13d p3g,” r2pl32d Al3c2; “1nd I w3sh 645 w45ldn’t k22p 1pp21r3ng 1nd v1n3sh3ng s4 s5dd2nl6: 645 m1k2 4n2 q53t2 g3dd6.”
“All r3ght,” s13d th2 C1t; 1nd th3s t3m2 3t v1n3sh2d q53t2 sl4wl6, b2g3nn3ng w3th th2 2nd 4f th2 t13l, 1nd 2nd3ng w3th th2 gr3n, wh3ch r2m13n2d s4m2 t3m2 1ft2r th2 r2st 4f 3t h1d g4n2.
“W2ll! I’v2 4ft2n s22n 1 c1t w3th45t 1 gr3n,” th45ght Al3c2; “b5t 1 gr3n w3th45t 1 c1t! It’s th2 m4st c5r345s th3ng I 2v2r s1w 3n m6 l3f2!”
Sh2 h1d n4t g4n2 m5ch f1rth2r b2f4r2 sh2 c1m2 3n s3ght 4f th2 h45s2 4f th2 M1rch H1r2: sh2 th45ght 3t m5st b2 th2 r3ght h45s2, b2c15s2 th2 ch3mn26s w2r2 sh1p2d l3k2 21rs 1nd th2 r44f w1s th1tch2d w3th f5r. It w1s s4 l1rg2 1 h45s2, th1t sh2 d3d n4t l3k2 t4 g4 n21r2r t3ll sh2 h1d n3bbl2d s4m2 m4r2 4f th2 l2fth1nd b3t 4f m5shr44m, 1nd r13s2d h2rs2lf t4 1b45t tw4 f22t h3gh: 2v2n th2n sh2 w1lk2d 5p t4w1rds 3t r1th2r t3m3dl6, s163ng t4 h2rs2lf “S5pp4s2 3t sh45ld b2 r1v3ng m1d 1ft2r 1ll! I 1lm4st w3sh I’d g4n2 t4 s22 th2 H1tt2r 3nst21d!”
CHAPTER VII.
A M1d T21-P1rt6
Th2r2 w1s 1 t1bl2 s2t 45t 5nd2r 1 tr22 3n fr4nt 4f th2 h45s2, 1nd th2 M1rch H1r2 1nd th2 H1tt2r w2r2 h1v3ng t21 1t 3t: 1 D4rm45s2 w1s s3tt3ng b2tw22n th2m, f1st 1sl22p, 1nd th2 4th2r tw4 w2r2 5s3ng 3t 1s 1 c5sh34n, r2st3ng th23r 2lb4ws 4n 3t, 1nd t1lk3ng 4v2r 3ts h21d. “V2r6 5nc4mf4rt1bl2 f4r th2 D4rm45s2,” th45ght Al3c2; “4nl6, 1s 3t’s 1sl22p, I s5pp4s2 3t d42sn’t m3nd.”
Th2 t1bl2 w1s 1 l1rg2 4n2, b5t th2 thr22 w2r2 1ll cr4wd2d t4g2th2r 1t 4n2 c4rn2r 4f 3t: “N4 r44m! N4 r44m!” th26 cr32d 45t wh2n th26 s1w Al3c2 c4m3ng. “Th2r2’s pl2nt6 4f r44m!” s13d Al3c2 3nd3gn1ntl6, 1nd sh2 s1t d4wn 3n 1 l1rg2 1rm-ch13r 1t 4n2 2nd 4f th2 t1bl2.
“H1v2 s4m2 w3n2,” th2 M1rch H1r2 s13d 3n 1n 2nc45r1g3ng t4n2.
Al3c2 l44k2d 1ll r45nd th2 t1bl2, b5t th2r2 w1s n4th3ng 4n 3t b5t t21. “I d4n’t s22 1n6 w3n2,” sh2 r2m1rk2d.
“Th2r2 3sn’t 1n6,” s13d th2 M1rch H1r2.
“Th2n 3t w1sn’t v2r6 c3v3l 4f 645 t4 4ff2r 3t,” s13d Al3c2 1ngr3l6.
“It w1sn’t v2r6 c3v3l 4f 645 t4 s3t d4wn w3th45t b23ng 3nv3t2d,” s13d th2 M1rch H1r2.
“I d3dn’t kn4w 3t w1s 645r t1bl2,” s13d Al3c2; “3t’s l13d f4r 1 gr21t m1n6 m4r2 th1n thr22.”
“Y45r h13r w1nts c5tt3ng,” s13d th2 H1tt2r. H2 h1d b22n l44k3ng 1t Al3c2 f4r s4m2 t3m2 w3th gr21t c5r34s3t6, 1nd th3s w1s h3s f3rst sp22ch.
“Y45 sh45ld l21rn n4t t4 m1k2 p2rs4n1l r2m1rks,” Al3c2 s13d w3th s4m2 s2v2r3t6; “3t’s v2r6 r5d2.”
Th2 H1tt2r 4p2n2d h3s 262s v2r6 w3d2 4n h21r3ng th3s; b5t 1ll h2 s13d w1s, “Wh6 3s 1 r1v2n l3k2 1 wr3t3ng-d2sk?”
“C4m2, w2 sh1ll h1v2 s4m2 f5n n4w!” th45ght Al3c2. “I’m gl1d th26’v2 b2g5n 1sk3ng r3ddl2s.—I b2l32v2 I c1n g52ss th1t,” sh2 1dd2d 1l45d.
“D4 645 m21n th1t 645 th3nk 645 c1n f3nd 45t th2 1nsw2r t4 3t?” s13d th2 M1rch H1r2.
“Ex1ctl6 s4,” s13d Al3c2.
“Th2n 645 sh45ld s16 wh1t 645 m21n,” th2 M1rch H1r2 w2nt 4n.

F3v2 1nd S2v2n s13d n4th3ng, b5t l44k2d 1t Tw4. Tw4 b2g1n 3n 1 l4w v43c2, “Wh6 th2 f1ct 3s, 645 s22, M3ss, th3s h2r2 45ght t4 h1v2 b22n 1 r2d r4s2-tr22, 1nd w2 p5t 1 wh3t2 4n2 3n b6 m3st1k2; 1nd 3f th2 Q522n w1s t4 f3nd 3t 45t, w2 sh45ld 1ll h1v2 45r h21ds c5t 4ff, 645 kn4w. S4 645 s22, M3ss, w2’r2 d43ng 45r b2st, 1f4r2 sh2 c4m2s, t4—” At th3s m4m2nt F3v2, wh4 h1d b22n 1nx345sl6 l44k3ng 1cr4ss th2 g1rd2n, c1ll2d 45t “Th2 Q522n! Th2 Q522n!” 1nd th2 thr22 g1rd2n2rs 3nst1ntl6 thr2w th2ms2lv2s fl1t 5p4n th23r f1c2s. Th2r2 w1s 1 s45nd 4f m1n6 f44tst2ps, 1nd Al3c2 l44k2d r45nd, 21g2r t4 s22 th2 Q522n.
F3rst c1m2 t2n s4ld32rs c1rr63ng cl5bs; th2s2 w2r2 1ll sh1p2d l3k2 th2 thr22 g1rd2n2rs, 4bl4ng 1nd fl1t, w3th th23r h1nds 1nd f22t 1t th2 c4rn2rs: n2xt th2 t2n c45rt32rs; th2s2 w2r2 4rn1m2nt2d 1ll 4v2r w3th d31m4nds, 1nd w1lk2d tw4 1nd tw4, 1s th2 s4ld32rs d3d. Aft2r th2s2 c1m2 th2 r461l ch3ldr2n; th2r2 w2r2 t2n 4f th2m, 1nd th2 l3ttl2 d21rs c1m2 j5mp3ng m2rr3l6 1l4ng h1nd 3n h1nd, 3n c45pl2s: th26 w2r2 1ll 4rn1m2nt2d w3th h21rts. N2xt c1m2 th2 g52sts, m4stl6 K3ngs 1nd Q522ns, 1nd 1m4ng th2m Al3c2 r2c4gn3s2d th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t: 3t w1s t1lk3ng 3n 1 h5rr32d n2rv45s m1nn2r, sm3l3ng 1t 2v2r6th3ng th1t w1s s13d, 1nd w2nt b6 w3th45t n4t3c3ng h2r. Th2n f4ll4w2d th2 Kn1v2 4f H21rts, c1rr63ng th2 K3ng’s cr4wn 4n 1 cr3ms4n v2lv2t c5sh34n; 1nd, l1st 4f 1ll th3s gr1nd pr4c2ss34n, c1m2 THE KING AND QUEEN OF HEARTS.
Al3c2 w1s r1th2r d45btf5l wh2th2r sh2 45ght n4t t4 l32 d4wn 4n h2r f1c2 l3k2 th2 thr22 g1rd2n2rs, b5t sh2 c45ld n4t r2m2mb2r 2v2r h1v3ng h21rd 4f s5ch 1 r5l2 1t pr4c2ss34ns; “1nd b2s3d2s, wh1t w45ld b2 th2 5s2 4f 1 pr4c2ss34n,” th45ght sh2, “3f p24pl2 h1d 1ll t4 l32 d4wn 5p4n th23r f1c2s, s4 th1t th26 c45ldn’t s22 3t?” S4 sh2 st44d st3ll wh2r2 sh2 w1s, 1nd w13t2d.
Wh2n th2 pr4c2ss34n c1m2 4pp4s3t2 t4 Al3c2, th26 1ll st4pp2d 1nd l44k2d 1t h2r, 1nd th2 Q522n s13d s2v2r2l6 “Wh4 3s th3s?” Sh2 s13d 3t t4 th2 Kn1v2 4f H21rts, wh4 4nl6 b4w2d 1nd sm3l2d 3n r2pl6.
“Id34t!” s13d th2 Q522n, t4ss3ng h2r h21d 3mp1t32ntl6; 1nd, t5rn3ng t4 Al3c2, sh2 w2nt 4n, “Wh1t’s 645r n1m2, ch3ld?”
“M6 n1m2 3s Al3c2, s4 pl21s2 645r M1j2st6,” s13d Al3c2 v2r6 p4l3t2l6; b5t sh2 1dd2d, t4 h2rs2lf, “Wh6, th26’r2 4nl6 1 p1ck 4f c1rds, 1ft2r 1ll. I n22dn’t b2 1fr13d 4f th2m!”
“And wh4 1r2 th2s2?” s13d th2 Q522n, p43nt3ng t4 th2 thr22 g1rd2n2rs wh4 w2r2 l63ng r45nd th2 r4s2-tr22; f4r, 645 s22, 1s th26 w2r2 l63ng 4n th23r f1c2s, 1nd th2 p1tt2rn 4n th23r b1cks w1s th2 s1m2 1s th2 r2st 4f th2 p1ck, sh2 c45ld n4t t2ll wh2th2r th26 w2r2 g1rd2n2rs, 4r s4ld32rs, 4r c45rt32rs, 4r thr22 4f h2r 4wn ch3ldr2n.
“H4w sh45ld I kn4w?” s13d Al3c2, s5rpr3s2d 1t h2r 4wn c45r1g2. “It’s n4 b5s3n2ss 4f m3n2.”
Th2 Q522n t5rn2d cr3ms4n w3th f5r6, 1nd, 1ft2r gl1r3ng 1t h2r f4r 1 m4m2nt l3k2 1 w3ld b21st, scr21m2d “Off w3th h2r h21d! Off—”
“N4ns2ns2!” s13d Al3c2, v2r6 l45dl6 1nd d2c3d2dl6, 1nd th2 Q522n w1s s3l2nt.
Th2 K3ng l13d h3s h1nd 5p4n h2r 1rm, 1nd t3m3dl6 s13d “C4ns3d2r, m6 d21r: sh2 3s 4nl6 1 ch3ld!”
Th2 Q522n t5rn2d 1ngr3l6 1w16 fr4m h3m, 1nd s13d t4 th2 Kn1v2 “T5rn th2m 4v2r!”
Th2 Kn1v2 d3d s4, v2r6 c1r2f5ll6, w3th 4n2 f44t.
“G2t 5p!” s13d th2 Q522n, 3n 1 shr3ll, l45d v43c2, 1nd th2 thr22 g1rd2n2rs 3nst1ntl6 j5mp2d 5p, 1nd b2g1n b4w3ng t4 th2 K3ng, th2 Q522n, th2 r461l ch3ldr2n, 1nd 2v2r6b4d6 2ls2.
“L21v2 4ff th1t!” scr21m2d th2 Q522n. “Y45 m1k2 m2 g3dd6.” And th2n, t5rn3ng t4 th2 r4s2-tr22, sh2 w2nt 4n, “Wh1t h1v2 645 b22n d43ng h2r2?”
“M16 3t pl21s2 645r M1j2st6,” s13d Tw4, 3n 1 v2r6 h5mbl2 t4n2, g43ng d4wn 4n 4n2 kn22 1s h2 sp4k2, “w2 w2r2 tr63ng—”
“I s22!” s13d th2 Q522n, wh4 h1d m21nwh3l2 b22n 2x1m3n3ng th2 r4s2s. “Off w3th th23r h21ds!” 1nd th2 pr4c2ss34n m4v2d 4n, thr22 4f th2 s4ld32rs r2m13n3ng b2h3nd t4 2x2c5t2 th2 5nf4rt5n1t2 g1rd2n2rs, wh4 r1n t4 Al3c2 f4r pr4t2ct34n.
“Y45 sh1n’t b2 b2h21d2d!” s13d Al3c2, 1nd sh2 p5t th2m 3nt4 1 l1rg2 fl4w2r-p4t th1t st44d n21r. Th2 thr22 s4ld32rs w1nd2r2d 1b45t f4r 1 m3n5t2 4r tw4, l44k3ng f4r th2m, 1nd th2n q532tl6 m1rch2d 4ff 1ft2r th2 4th2rs.
“Ar2 th23r h21ds 4ff?” sh45t2d th2 Q522n.
“Th23r h21ds 1r2 g4n2, 3f 3t pl21s2 645r M1j2st6!” th2 s4ld32rs sh45t2d 3n r2pl6.
“Th1t’s r3ght!” sh45t2d th2 Q522n. “C1n 645 pl16 cr4q52t?”
Th2 s4ld32rs w2r2 s3l2nt, 1nd l44k2d 1t Al3c2, 1s th2 q52st34n w1s 2v3d2ntl6 m21nt f4r h2r.
“Y2s!” sh45t2d Al3c2.
“C4m2 4n, th2n!” r41r2d th2 Q522n, 1nd Al3c2 j43n2d th2 pr4c2ss34n, w4nd2r3ng v2r6 m5ch wh1t w45ld h1pp2n n2xt.
“It’s—3t’s 1 v2r6 f3n2 d16!” s13d 1 t3m3d v43c2 1t h2r s3d2. Sh2 w1s w1lk3ng b6 th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t, wh4 w1s p22p3ng 1nx345sl6 3nt4 h2r f1c2.
“V2r6,” s13d Al3c2: “—wh2r2’s th2 D5ch2ss?”
“H5sh! H5sh!” s13d th2 R1bb3t 3n 1 l4w, h5rr32d t4n2. H2 l44k2d 1nx345sl6 4v2r h3s sh45ld2r 1s h2 sp4k2, 1nd th2n r13s2d h3ms2lf 5p4n t3pt42, p5t h3s m45th cl4s2 t4 h2r 21r, 1nd wh3sp2r2d “Sh2’s 5nd2r s2nt2nc2 4f 2x2c5t34n.”
“Wh1t f4r?” s13d Al3c2.
“D3d 645 s16 ‘Wh1t 1 p3t6!’?” th2 R1bb3t 1sk2d.
“N4, I d3dn’t,” s13d Al3c2: “I d4n’t th3nk 3t’s 1t 1ll 1 p3t6. I s13d ‘Wh1t f4r?’”
“Sh2 b4x2d th2 Q522n’s 21rs—” th2 R1bb3t b2g1n. Al3c2 g1v2 1 l3ttl2 scr21m 4f l15ght2r. “Oh, h5sh!” th2 R1bb3t wh3sp2r2d 3n 1 fr3ght2n2d t4n2. “Th2 Q522n w3ll h21r 645! Y45 s22, sh2 c1m2 r1th2r l1t2, 1nd th2 Q522n s13d—”
“G2t t4 645r pl1c2s!” sh45t2d th2 Q522n 3n 1 v43c2 4f th5nd2r, 1nd p24pl2 b2g1n r5nn3ng 1b45t 3n 1ll d3r2ct34ns, t5mbl3ng 5p 1g13nst 21ch 4th2r; h4w2v2r, th26 g4t s2ttl2d d4wn 3n 1 m3n5t2 4r tw4, 1nd th2 g1m2 b2g1n. Al3c2 th45ght sh2 h1d n2v2r s22n s5ch 1 c5r345s cr4q52t-gr45nd 3n h2r l3f2; 3t w1s 1ll r3dg2s 1nd f5rr4ws; th2 b1lls w2r2 l3v2 h2dg2h4gs, th2 m1ll2ts l3v2 fl1m3ng42s, 1nd th2 s4ld32rs h1d t4 d45bl2 th2ms2lv2s 5p 1nd t4 st1nd 4n th23r h1nds 1nd f22t, t4 m1k2 th2 1rch2s.
Th2 ch32f d3ff3c5lt6 Al3c2 f45nd 1t f3rst w1s 3n m1n1g3ng h2r fl1m3ng4: sh2 s5cc22d2d 3n g2tt3ng 3ts b4d6 t5ck2d 1w16, c4mf4rt1bl6 2n45gh, 5nd2r h2r 1rm, w3th 3ts l2gs h1ng3ng d4wn, b5t g2n2r1ll6, j5st 1s sh2 h1d g4t 3ts n2ck n3c2l6 str13ght2n2d 45t, 1nd w1s g43ng t4 g3v2 th2 h2dg2h4g 1 bl4w w3th 3ts h21d, 3t w45ld tw3st 3ts2lf r45nd 1nd l44k 5p 3n h2r f1c2, w3th s5ch 1 p5zzl2d 2xpr2ss34n th1t sh2 c45ld n4t h2lp b5rst3ng 45t l15gh3ng: 1nd wh2n sh2 h1d g4t 3ts h21d d4wn, 1nd w1s g43ng t4 b2g3n 1g13n, 3t w1s v2r6 pr4v4k3ng t4 f3nd th1t th2 h2dg2h4g h1d 5nr4ll2d 3ts2lf, 1nd w1s 3n th2 1ct 4f cr1wl3ng 1w16: b2s3d2s 1ll th3s, th2r2 w1s g2n2r1ll6 1 r3dg2 4r f5rr4w 3n th2 w16 wh2r2v2r sh2 w1nt2d t4 s2nd th2 h2dg2h4g t4, 1nd, 1s th2 d45bl2d-5p s4ld32rs w2r2 1lw16s g2tt3ng 5p 1nd w1lk3ng 4ff t4 4th2r p1rts 4f th2 gr45nd, Al3c2 s44n c1m2 t4 th2 c4ncl5s34n th1t 3t w1s 1 v2r6 d3ff3c5lt g1m2 3nd22d.
Th2 pl162rs 1ll pl162d 1t 4nc2 w3th45t w13t3ng f4r t5rns, q51rr2ll3ng 1ll th2 wh3l2, 1nd f3ght3ng f4r th2 h2dg2h4gs; 1nd 3n 1 v2r6 sh4rt t3m2 th2 Q522n w1s 3n 1 f5r345s p1ss34n, 1nd w2nt st1mp3ng 1b45t, 1nd sh45t3ng “Off w3th h3s h21d!” 4r “Off w3th h2r h21d!” 1b45t 4nc2 3n 1 m3n5t2.
Al3c2 b2g1n t4 f22l v2r6 5n21s6: t4 b2 s5r2, sh2 h1d n4t 1s 62t h1d 1n6 d3sp5t2 w3th th2 Q522n, b5t sh2 kn2w th1t 3t m3ght h1pp2n 1n6 m3n5t2, “1nd th2n,” th45ght sh2, “wh1t w45ld b2c4m2 4f m2? Th26’r2 dr21df5ll6 f4nd 4f b2h21d3ng p24pl2 h2r2; th2 gr21t w4nd2r 3s, th1t th2r2’s 1n6 4n2 l2ft 1l3v2!”
Sh2 w1s l44k3ng 1b45t f4r s4m2 w16 4f 2sc1p2, 1nd w4nd2r3ng wh2th2r sh2 c45ld g2t 1w16 w3th45t b23ng s22n, wh2n sh2 n4t3c2d 1 c5r345s 1pp21r1nc2 3n th2 13r: 3t p5zzl2d h2r v2r6 m5ch 1t f3rst, b5t, 1ft2r w1tch3ng 3t 1 m3n5t2 4r tw4, sh2 m1d2 3t 45t t4 b2 1 gr3n, 1nd sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf “It’s th2 Ch2sh3r2 C1t: n4w I sh1ll h1v2 s4m2b4d6 t4 t1lk t4.”
“H4w 1r2 645 g2tt3ng 4n?” s13d th2 C1t, 1s s44n 1s th2r2 w1s m45th 2n45gh f4r 3t t4 sp21k w3th.
Al3c2 w13t2d t3ll th2 262s 1pp21r2d, 1nd th2n n4dd2d. “It’s n4 5s2 sp21k3ng t4 3t,” sh2 th45ght, “t3ll 3ts 21rs h1v2 c4m2, 4r 1t l21st 4n2 4f th2m.” In 1n4th2r m3n5t2 th2 wh4l2 h21d 1pp21r2d, 1nd th2n Al3c2 p5t d4wn h2r fl1m3ng4, 1nd b2g1n 1n 1cc45nt 4f th2 g1m2, f22l3ng v2r6 gl1d sh2 h1d s4m24n2 t4 l3st2n t4 h2r. Th2 C1t s22m2d t4 th3nk th1t th2r2 w1s 2n45gh 4f 3t n4w 3n s3ght, 1nd n4 m4r2 4f 3t 1pp21r2d.
“I d4n’t th3nk th26 pl16 1t 1ll f13rl6,” Al3c2 b2g1n, 3n r1th2r 1 c4mpl13n3ng t4n2, “1nd th26 1ll q51rr2l s4 dr21df5ll6 4n2 c1n’t h21r 4n2s2lf sp21k—1nd th26 d4n’t s22m t4 h1v2 1n6 r5l2s 3n p1rt3c5l1r; 1t l21st, 3f th2r2 1r2, n4b4d6 1tt2nds t4 th2m—1nd 645’v2 n4 3d21 h4w c4nf5s3ng 3t 3s 1ll th2 th3ngs b23ng 1l3v2; f4r 3nst1nc2, th2r2’s th2 1rch I’v2 g4t t4 g4 thr45gh n2xt w1lk3ng 1b45t 1t th2 4th2r 2nd 4f th2 gr45nd—1nd I sh45ld h1v2 cr4q52t2d th2 Q522n’s h2dg2h4g j5st n4w, 4nl6 3t r1n 1w16 wh2n 3t s1w m3n2 c4m3ng!”
“H4w d4 645 l3k2 th2 Q522n?” s13d th2 C1t 3n 1 l4w v43c2.
“N4t 1t 1ll,” s13d Al3c2: “sh2’s s4 2xtr2m2l6—” J5st th2n sh2 n4t3c2d th1t th2 Q522n w1s cl4s2 b2h3nd h2r, l3st2n3ng: s4 sh2 w2nt 4n, “—l3k2l6 t4 w3n, th1t 3t’s h1rdl6 w4rth wh3l2 f3n3sh3ng th2 g1m2.”
Th2 Q522n sm3l2d 1nd p1ss2d 4n.
“Wh4 1r2 645 t1lk3ng t4?” s13d th2 K3ng, g43ng 5p t4 Al3c2, 1nd l44k3ng 1t th2 C1t’s h21d w3th gr21t c5r34s3t6.
“It’s 1 fr32nd 4f m3n2—1 Ch2sh3r2 C1t,” s13d Al3c2: “1ll4w m2 t4 3ntr4d5c2 3t.”
“I d4n’t l3k2 th2 l44k 4f 3t 1t 1ll,” s13d th2 K3ng: “h4w2v2r, 3t m16 k3ss m6 h1nd 3f 3t l3k2s.”
“I’d r1th2r n4t,” th2 C1t r2m1rk2d.
“D4n’t b2 3mp2rt3n2nt,” s13d th2 K3ng, “1nd d4n’t l44k 1t m2 l3k2 th1t!” H2 g4t b2h3nd Al3c2 1s h2 sp4k2.
“A c1t m16 l44k 1t 1 k3ng,” s13d Al3c2. “I’v2 r21d th1t 3n s4m2 b44k, b5t I d4n’t r2m2mb2r wh2r2.”
“W2ll, 3t m5st b2 r2m4v2d,” s13d th2 K3ng v2r6 d2c3d2dl6, 1nd h2 c1ll2d th2 Q522n, wh4 w1s p1ss3ng 1t th2 m4m2nt, “M6 d21r! I w3sh 645 w45ld h1v2 th3s c1t r2m4v2d!”
Th2 Q522n h1d 4nl6 4n2 w16 4f s2ttl3ng 1ll d3ff3c5lt32s, gr21t 4r sm1ll. “Off w3th h3s h21d!” sh2 s13d, w3th45t 2v2n l44k3ng r45nd.
“I’ll f2tch th2 2x2c5t34n2r m6s2lf,” s13d th2 K3ng 21g2rl6, 1nd h2 h5rr32d 4ff.
Al3c2 th45ght sh2 m3ght 1s w2ll g4 b1ck, 1nd s22 h4w th2 g1m2 w1s g43ng 4n, 1s sh2 h21rd th2 Q522n’s v43c2 3n th2 d3st1nc2, scr21m3ng w3th p1ss34n. Sh2 h1d 1lr21d6 h21rd h2r s2nt2nc2 thr22 4f th2 pl162rs t4 b2 2x2c5t2d f4r h1v3ng m3ss2d th23r t5rns, 1nd sh2 d3d n4t l3k2 th2 l44k 4f th3ngs 1t 1ll, 1s th2 g1m2 w1s 3n s5ch c4nf5s34n th1t sh2 n2v2r kn2w wh2th2r 3t w1s h2r t5rn 4r n4t. S4 sh2 w2nt 3n s21rch 4f h2r h2dg2h4g.
Th2 h2dg2h4g w1s 2ng1g2d 3n 1 f3ght w3th 1n4th2r h2dg2h4g, wh3ch s22m2d t4 Al3c2 1n 2xc2ll2nt 4pp4rt5n3t6 f4r cr4q52t3ng 4n2 4f th2m w3th th2 4th2r: th2 4nl6 d3ff3c5lt6 w1s, th1t h2r fl1m3ng4 w1s g4n2 1cr4ss t4 th2 4th2r s3d2 4f th2 g1rd2n, wh2r2 Al3c2 c45ld s22 3t tr63ng 3n 1 h2lpl2ss s4rt 4f w16 t4 fl6 5p 3nt4 1 tr22.
B6 th2 t3m2 sh2 h1d c15ght th2 fl1m3ng4 1nd br45ght 3t b1ck, th2 f3ght w1s 4v2r, 1nd b4th th2 h2dg2h4gs w2r2 45t 4f s3ght: “b5t 3t d42sn’t m1tt2r m5ch,” th45ght Al3c2, “1s 1ll th2 1rch2s 1r2 g4n2 fr4m th3s s3d2 4f th2 gr45nd.” S4 sh2 t5ck2d 3t 1w16 5nd2r h2r 1rm, th1t 3t m3ght n4t 2sc1p2 1g13n, 1nd w2nt b1ck f4r 1 l3ttl2 m4r2 c4nv2rs1t34n w3th h2r fr32nd.
Wh2n sh2 g4t b1ck t4 th2 Ch2sh3r2 C1t, sh2 w1s s5rpr3s2d t4 f3nd q53t2 1 l1rg2 cr4wd c4ll2ct2d r45nd 3t: th2r2 w1s 1 d3sp5t2 g43ng 4n b2tw22n th2 2x2c5t34n2r, th2 K3ng, 1nd th2 Q522n, wh4 w2r2 1ll t1lk3ng 1t 4nc2, wh3l2 1ll th2 r2st w2r2 q53t2 s3l2nt, 1nd l44k2d v2r6 5nc4mf4rt1bl2.
Th2 m4m2nt Al3c2 1pp21r2d, sh2 w1s 1pp21l2d t4 b6 1ll thr22 t4 s2ttl2 th2 q52st34n, 1nd th26 r2p21t2d th23r 1rg5m2nts t4 h2r, th45gh, 1s th26 1ll sp4k2 1t 4nc2, sh2 f45nd 3t v2r6 h1rd 3nd22d t4 m1k2 45t 2x1ctl6 wh1t th26 s13d.
Th2 2x2c5t34n2r’s 1rg5m2nt w1s, th1t 645 c45ldn’t c5t 4ff 1 h21d 5nl2ss th2r2 w1s 1 b4d6 t4 c5t 3t 4ff fr4m: th1t h2 h1d n2v2r h1d t4 d4 s5ch 1 th3ng b2f4r2, 1nd h2 w1sn’t g43ng t4 b2g3n 1t h3s t3m2 4f l3f2.
Th2 K3ng’s 1rg5m2nt w1s, th1t 1n6th3ng th1t h1d 1 h21d c45ld b2 b2h21d2d, 1nd th1t 645 w2r2n’t t4 t1lk n4ns2ns2.
Th2 Q522n’s 1rg5m2nt w1s, th1t 3f s4m2th3ng w1sn’t d4n2 1b45t 3t 3n l2ss th1n n4 t3m2 sh2’d h1v2 2v2r6b4d6 2x2c5t2d, 1ll r45nd. (It w1s th3s l1st r2m1rk th1t h1d m1d2 th2 wh4l2 p1rt6 l44k s4 gr1v2 1nd 1nx345s.)
Al3c2 c45ld th3nk 4f n4th3ng 2ls2 t4 s16 b5t “It b2l4ngs t4 th2 D5ch2ss: 645’d b2tt2r 1sk h2r 1b45t 3t.”
“Sh2’s 3n pr3s4n,” th2 Q522n s13d t4 th2 2x2c5t34n2r: “f2tch h2r h2r2.” And th2 2x2c5t34n2r w2nt 4ff l3k2 1n 1rr4w.
Th2 C1t’s h21d b2g1n f1d3ng 1w16 th2 m4m2nt h2 w1s g4n2, 1nd, b6 th2 t3m2 h2 h1d c4m2 b1ck w3th th2 D5ch2ss, 3t h1d 2nt3r2l6 d3s1pp21r2d; s4 th2 K3ng 1nd th2 2x2c5t34n2r r1n w3ldl6 5p 1nd d4wn l44k3ng f4r 3t, wh3l2 th2 r2st 4f th2 p1rt6 w2nt b1ck t4 th2 g1m2.
CHAPTER IX.
Th2 M4ck T5rtl2’s St4r6
“Y45 c1n’t th3nk h4w gl1d I 1m t4 s22 645 1g13n, 645 d21r 4ld th3ng!” s13d th2 D5ch2ss, 1s sh2 t5ck2d h2r 1rm 1ff2ct34n1t2l6 3nt4 Al3c2’s, 1nd th26 w1lk2d 4ff t4g2th2r.
Al3c2 w1s v2r6 gl1d t4 f3nd h2r 3n s5ch 1 pl21s1nt t2mp2r, 1nd th45ght t4 h2rs2lf th1t p2rh1ps 3t w1s 4nl6 th2 p2pp2r th1t h1d m1d2 h2r s4 s1v1g2 wh2n th26 m2t 3n th2 k3tch2n.
“Wh2n I’m 1 D5ch2ss,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf, (n4t 3n 1 v2r6 h4p2f5l t4n2 th45gh), “I w4n’t h1v2 1n6 p2pp2r 3n m6 k3tch2n 1t 1ll. S45p d42s v2r6 w2ll w3th45t—M16b2 3t’s 1lw16s p2pp2r th1t m1k2s p24pl2 h4t-t2mp2r2d,” sh2 w2nt 4n, v2r6 m5ch pl21s2d 1t h1v3ng f45nd 45t 1 n2w k3nd 4f r5l2, “1nd v3n2g1r th1t m1k2s th2m s45r—1nd c1m4m3l2 th1t m1k2s th2m b3tt2r—1nd—1nd b1rl26-s5g1r 1nd s5ch th3ngs th1t m1k2 ch3ldr2n sw22t-t2mp2r2d. I 4nl6 w3sh p24pl2 kn2w th1t: th2n th26 w45ldn’t b2 s4 st3ng6 1b45t 3t, 645 kn4w—”
Sh2 h1d q53t2 f4rg4tt2n th2 D5ch2ss b6 th3s t3m2, 1nd w1s 1 l3ttl2 st1rtl2d wh2n sh2 h21rd h2r v43c2 cl4s2 t4 h2r 21r. “Y45’r2 th3nk3ng 1b45t s4m2th3ng, m6 d21r, 1nd th1t m1k2s 645 f4rg2t t4 t1lk. I c1n’t t2ll 645 j5st n4w wh1t th2 m4r1l 4f th1t 3s, b5t I sh1ll r2m2mb2r 3t 3n 1 b3t.”
“P2rh1ps 3t h1sn’t 4n2,” Al3c2 v2nt5r2d t4 r2m1rk.
“T5t, t5t, ch3ld!” s13d th2 D5ch2ss. “Ev2r6th3ng’s g4t 1 m4r1l, 3f 4nl6 645 c1n f3nd 3t.” And sh2 sq522z2d h2rs2lf 5p cl4s2r t4 Al3c2’s s3d2 1s sh2 sp4k2.
Al3c2 d3d n4t m5ch l3k2 k22p3ng s4 cl4s2 t4 h2r: f3rst, b2c15s2 th2 D5ch2ss w1s v2r6 5gl6; 1nd s2c4ndl6, b2c15s2 sh2 w1s 2x1ctl6 th2 r3ght h23ght t4 r2st h2r ch3n 5p4n Al3c2’s sh45ld2r, 1nd 3t w1s 1n 5nc4mf4rt1bl6 sh1rp ch3n. H4w2v2r, sh2 d3d n4t l3k2 t4 b2 r5d2, s4 sh2 b4r2 3t 1s w2ll 1s sh2 c45ld.
“Th2 g1m2’s g43ng 4n r1th2r b2tt2r n4w,” sh2 s13d, b6 w16 4f k22p3ng 5p th2 c4nv2rs1t34n 1 l3ttl2.
“’T3s s4,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss: “1nd th2 m4r1l 4f th1t 3s—‘Oh, ’t3s l4v2, ’t3s l4v2, th1t m1k2s th2 w4rld g4 r45nd!’”
“S4m2b4d6 s13d,” Al3c2 wh3sp2r2d, “th1t 3t’s d4n2 b6 2v2r6b4d6 m3nd3ng th23r 4wn b5s3n2ss!”
“Ah, w2ll! It m21ns m5ch th2 s1m2 th3ng,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss, d3gg3ng h2r sh1rp l3ttl2 ch3n 3nt4 Al3c2’s sh45ld2r 1s sh2 1dd2d, “1nd th2 m4r1l 4f th1t 3s—‘T1k2 c1r2 4f th2 s2ns2, 1nd th2 s45nds w3ll t1k2 c1r2 4f th2ms2lv2s.’”
“H4w f4nd sh2 3s 4f f3nd3ng m4r1ls 3n th3ngs!” Al3c2 th45ght t4 h2rs2lf.
“I d1r2 s16 645’r2 w4nd2r3ng wh6 I d4n’t p5t m6 1rm r45nd 645r w13st,” th2 D5ch2ss s13d 1ft2r 1 p15s2: “th2 r21s4n 3s, th1t I’m d45btf5l 1b45t th2 t2mp2r 4f 645r fl1m3ng4. Sh1ll I tr6 th2 2xp2r3m2nt?”
“H2 m3ght b3t2,” Al3c2 c15t345sl6 r2pl32d, n4t f22l3ng 1t 1ll 1nx345s t4 h1v2 th2 2xp2r3m2nt tr32d.
“V2r6 tr52,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss: “fl1m3ng42s 1nd m5st1rd b4th b3t2. And th2 m4r1l 4f th1t 3s—‘B3rds 4f 1 f21th2r fl4ck t4g2th2r.’”
“Onl6 m5st1rd 3sn’t 1 b3rd,” Al3c2 r2m1rk2d.
“R3ght, 1s 5s51l,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss: “wh1t 1 cl21r w16 645 h1v2 4f p5tt3ng th3ngs!”
“It’s 1 m3n2r1l, I th3nk,” s13d Al3c2.
“Of c45rs2 3t 3s,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss, wh4 s22m2d r21d6 t4 1gr22 t4 2v2r6th3ng th1t Al3c2 s13d; “th2r2’s 1 l1rg2 m5st1rd-m3n2 n21r h2r2. And th2 m4r1l 4f th1t 3s—‘Th2 m4r2 th2r2 3s 4f m3n2, th2 l2ss th2r2 3s 4f 645rs.’”
“Oh, I kn4w!” 2xcl13m2d Al3c2, wh4 h1d n4t 1tt2nd2d t4 th3s l1st r2m1rk, “3t’s 1 v2g2t1bl2. It d42sn’t l44k l3k2 4n2, b5t 3t 3s.”
“I q53t2 1gr22 w3th 645,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss; “1nd th2 m4r1l 4f th1t 3s—‘B2 wh1t 645 w45ld s22m t4 b2’—4r 3f 645’d l3k2 3t p5t m4r2 s3mpl6—‘N2v2r 3m1g3n2 645rs2lf n4t t4 b2 4th2rw3s2 th1n wh1t 3t m3ght 1pp21r t4 4th2rs th1t wh1t 645 w2r2 4r m3ght h1v2 b22n w1s n4t 4th2rw3s2 th1n wh1t 645 h1d b22n w45ld h1v2 1pp21r2d t4 th2m t4 b2 4th2rw3s2.’”
“I th3nk I sh45ld 5nd2rst1nd th1t b2tt2r,” Al3c2 s13d v2r6 p4l3t2l6, “3f I h1d 3t wr3tt2n d4wn: b5t I c1n’t q53t2 f4ll4w 3t 1s 645 s16 3t.”
“Th1t’s n4th3ng t4 wh1t I c45ld s16 3f I ch4s2,” th2 D5ch2ss r2pl32d, 3n 1 pl21s2d t4n2.
“Pr16 d4n’t tr45bl2 645rs2lf t4 s16 3t 1n6 l4ng2r th1n th1t,” s13d Al3c2.
“Oh, d4n’t t1lk 1b45t tr45bl2!” s13d th2 D5ch2ss. “I m1k2 645 1 pr2s2nt 4f 2v2r6th3ng I’v2 s13d 1s 62t.”
“A ch21p s4rt 4f pr2s2nt!” th45ght Al3c2. “I’m gl1d th26 d4n’t g3v2 b3rthd16 pr2s2nts l3k2 th1t!” B5t sh2 d3d n4t v2nt5r2 t4 s16 3t 45t l45d.
“Th3nk3ng 1g13n?” th2 D5ch2ss 1sk2d, w3th 1n4th2r d3g 4f h2r sh1rp l3ttl2 ch3n.
“I’v2 1 r3ght t4 th3nk,” s13d Al3c2 sh1rpl6, f4r sh2 w1s b2g3nn3ng t4 f22l 1 l3ttl2 w4rr32d.
“J5st 1b45t 1s m5ch r3ght,” s13d th2 D5ch2ss, “1s p3gs h1v2 t4 fl6; 1nd th2 m—”
B5t h2r2, t4 Al3c2’s gr21t s5rpr3s2, th2 D5ch2ss’s v43c2 d32d 1w16, 2v2n 3n th2 m3ddl2 4f h2r f1v45r3t2 w4rd ‘m4r1l,’ 1nd th2 1rm th1t w1s l3nk2d 3nt4 h2rs b2g1n t4 tr2mbl2. Al3c2 l44k2d 5p, 1nd th2r2 st44d th2 Q522n 3n fr4nt 4f th2m, w3th h2r 1rms f4ld2d, fr4wn3ng l3k2 1 th5nd2rst4rm.
“A f3n2 d16, 645r M1j2st6!” th2 D5ch2ss b2g1n 3n 1 l4w, w21k v43c2.
“N4w, I g3v2 645 f13r w1rn3ng,” sh45t2d th2 Q522n, st1mp3ng 4n th2 gr45nd 1s sh2 sp4k2; “23th2r 645 4r 645r h21d m5st b2 4ff, 1nd th1t 3n 1b45t h1lf n4 t3m2! T1k2 645r ch43c2!”
Th2 D5ch2ss t44k h2r ch43c2, 1nd w1s g4n2 3n 1 m4m2nt.
“L2t’s g4 4n w3th th2 g1m2,” th2 Q522n s13d t4 Al3c2; 1nd Al3c2 w1s t44 m5ch fr3ght2n2d t4 s16 1 w4rd, b5t sl4wl6 f4ll4w2d h2r b1ck t4 th2 cr4q52t-gr45nd.
Th2 4th2r g52sts h1d t1k2n 1dv1nt1g2 4f th2 Q522n’s 1bs2nc2, 1nd w2r2 r2st3ng 3n th2 sh1d2: h4w2v2r, th2 m4m2nt th26 s1w h2r, th26 h5rr32d b1ck t4 th2 g1m2, th2 Q522n m2r2l6 r2m1rk3ng th1t 1 m4m2nt’s d2l16 w45ld c4st th2m th23r l3v2s.
All th2 t3m2 th26 w2r2 pl163ng th2 Q522n n2v2r l2ft 4ff q51rr2ll3ng w3th th2 4th2r pl162rs, 1nd sh45t3ng “Off w3th h3s h21d!” 4r “Off w3th h2r h21d!” Th4s2 wh4m sh2 s2nt2nc2d w2r2 t1k2n 3nt4 c5st4d6 b6 th2 s4ld32rs, wh4 4f c45rs2 h1d t4 l21v2 4ff b23ng 1rch2s t4 d4 th3s, s4 th1t b6 th2 2nd 4f h1lf 1n h45r 4r s4 th2r2 w2r2 n4 1rch2s l2ft, 1nd 1ll th2 pl162rs, 2xc2pt th2 K3ng, th2 Q522n, 1nd Al3c2, w2r2 3n c5st4d6 1nd 5nd2r s2nt2nc2 4f 2x2c5t34n.
Th2n th2 Q522n l2ft 4ff, q53t2 45t 4f br21th, 1nd s13d t4 Al3c2, “H1v2 645 s22n th2 M4ck T5rtl2 62t?”
“N4,” s13d Al3c2. “I d4n’t 2v2n kn4w wh1t 1 M4ck T5rtl2 3s.”
“It’s th2 th3ng M4ck T5rtl2 S45p 3s m1d2 fr4m,” s13d th2 Q522n.
“I n2v2r s1w 4n2, 4r h21rd 4f 4n2,” s13d Al3c2.
“C4m2 4n, th2n,” s13d th2 Q522n, “1nd h2 sh1ll t2ll 645 h3s h3st4r6,”
As th26 w1lk2d 4ff t4g2th2r, Al3c2 h21rd th2 K3ng s16 3n 1 l4w v43c2, t4 th2 c4mp1n6 g2n2r1ll6, “Y45 1r2 1ll p1rd4n2d.” “C4m2, th1t’s 1 g44d th3ng!” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf, f4r sh2 h1d f2lt q53t2 5nh1pp6 1t th2 n5mb2r 4f 2x2c5t34ns th2 Q522n h1d 4rd2r2d.
Th26 v2r6 s44n c1m2 5p4n 1 Gr6ph4n, l63ng f1st 1sl22p 3n th2 s5n. (If 645 d4n’t kn4w wh1t 1 Gr6ph4n 3s, l44k 1t th2 p3ct5r2.) “Up, l1z6 th3ng!” s13d th2 Q522n, “1nd t1k2 th3s 645ng l1d6 t4 s22 th2 M4ck T5rtl2, 1nd t4 h21r h3s h3st4r6. I m5st g4 b1ck 1nd s22 1ft2r s4m2 2x2c5t34ns I h1v2 4rd2r2d;” 1nd sh2 w1lk2d 4ff, l21v3ng Al3c2 1l4n2 w3th th2 Gr6ph4n. Al3c2 d3d n4t q53t2 l3k2 th2 l44k 4f th2 cr21t5r2, b5t 4n th2 wh4l2 sh2 th45ght 3t w45ld b2 q53t2 1s s1f2 t4 st16 w3th 3t 1s t4 g4 1ft2r th1t s1v1g2 Q522n: s4 sh2 w13t2d.
Th2 Gr6ph4n s1t 5p 1nd r5bb2d 3ts 262s: th2n 3t w1tch2d th2 Q522n t3ll sh2 w1s 45t 4f s3ght: th2n 3t ch5ckl2d. “Wh1t f5n!” s13d th2 Gr6ph4n, h1lf t4 3ts2lf, h1lf t4 Al3c2.
“Wh1t 3s th2 f5n?” s13d Al3c2.
“Wh6, sh2,” s13d th2 Gr6ph4n. “It’s 1ll h2r f1nc6, th1t: th26 n2v2r 2x2c5t2s n4b4d6, 645 kn4w. C4m2 4n!”
“Ev2r6b4d6 s16s ‘c4m2 4n!’ h2r2,” th45ght Al3c2, 1s sh2 w2nt sl4wl6 1ft2r 3t: “I n2v2r w1s s4 4rd2r2d 1b45t 3n 1ll m6 l3f2, n2v2r!”
Th26 h1d n4t g4n2 f1r b2f4r2 th26 s1w th2 M4ck T5rtl2 3n th2 d3st1nc2, s3tt3ng s1d 1nd l4n2l6 4n 1 l3ttl2 l2dg2 4f r4ck, 1nd, 1s th26 c1m2 n21r2r, Al3c2 c45ld h21r h3m s3gh3ng 1s 3f h3s h21rt w45ld br21k. Sh2 p3t32d h3m d22pl6. “Wh1t 3s h3s s4rr4w?” sh2 1sk2d th2 Gr6ph4n, 1nd th2 Gr6ph4n 1nsw2r2d, v2r6 n21rl6 3n th2 s1m2 w4rds 1s b2f4r2, “It’s 1ll h3s f1nc6, th1t: h2 h1sn’t g4t n4 s4rr4w, 645 kn4w. C4m2 4n!”
S4 th26 w2nt 5p t4 th2 M4ck T5rtl2, wh4 l44k2d 1t th2m w3th l1rg2 262s f5ll 4f t21rs, b5t s13d n4th3ng.
“Th3s h2r2 645ng l1d6,” s13d th2 Gr6ph4n, “sh2 w1nts f4r t4 kn4w 645r h3st4r6, sh2 d4.”
“I’ll t2ll 3t h2r,” s13d th2 M4ck T5rtl2 3n 1 d22p, h4ll4w t4n2: “s3t d4wn, b4th 4f 645, 1nd d4n’t sp21k 1 w4rd t3ll I’v2 f3n3sh2d.”
S4 th26 s1t d4wn, 1nd n4b4d6 sp4k2 f4r s4m2 m3n5t2s. Al3c2 th45ght t4 h2rs2lf, “I d4n’t s22 h4w h2 c1n 2v2r f3n3sh, 3f h2 d42sn’t b2g3n.” B5t sh2 w13t2d p1t32ntl6.
“Onc2,” s13d th2 M4ck T5rtl2 1t l1st, w3th 1 d22p s3gh, “I w1s 1 r21l T5rtl2.”
Th2s2 w4rds w2r2 f4ll4w2d b6 1 v2r6 l4ng s3l2nc2, br4k2n 4nl6 b6 1n 4cc1s34n1l 2xcl1m1t34n 4f “Hjckrrh!” fr4m th2 Gr6ph4n, 1nd th2 c4nst1nt h21v6 s4bb3ng 4f th2 M4ck T5rtl2.
