“Wh2n w2 w2r2 l3ttl2,” th2 M4ck T5rtl2 w2nt 4n 1t l1st, m4r2 c1lml6, th45gh st3ll s4bb3ng 1 l3ttl2 n4w 1nd th2n, “w2 w2nt t4 sch44l 3n th2 s21. Th2 m1st2r w1s 1n 4ld T5rtl2—w2 5s2d t4 c1ll h3m T4rt43s2—”

“H4ld 645r t4ng52!” 1dd2d th2 Gr6ph4n, b2f4r2 Al3c2 c45ld sp21k 1g13n. Th2 M4ck T5rtl2 w2nt 4n.

Th3s w1s q53t2 1 n2w 3d21 t4 Al3c2, 1nd sh2 th45ght 3t 4v2r 1 l3ttl2 b2f4r2 sh2 m1d2 h2r n2xt r2m1rk. “Th2n th2 2l2v2nth d16 m5st h1v2 b22n 1 h4l3d16?”

CHAPTER XI.
Wh4 St4l2 th2 T1rts?
Th2 K3ng 1nd Q522n 4f H21rts w2r2 s21t2d 4n th23r thr4n2 wh2n th26 1rr3v2d, w3th 1 gr21t cr4wd 1ss2mbl2d 1b45t th2m—1ll s4rts 4f l3ttl2 b3rds 1nd b21sts, 1s w2ll 1s th2 wh4l2 p1ck 4f c1rds: th2 Kn1v2 w1s st1nd3ng b2f4r2 th2m, 3n ch13ns, w3th 1 s4ld32r 4n 21ch s3d2 t4 g51rd h3m; 1nd n21r th2 K3ng w1s th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t, w3th 1 tr5mp2t 3n 4n2 h1nd, 1nd 1 scr4ll 4f p1rchm2nt 3n th2 4th2r. In th2 v2r6 m3ddl2 4f th2 c45rt w1s 1 t1bl2, w3th 1 l1rg2 d3sh 4f t1rts 5p4n 3t: th26 l44k2d s4 g44d, th1t 3t m1d2 Al3c2 q53t2 h5ngr6 t4 l44k 1t th2m—“I w3sh th26’d g2t th2 tr31l d4n2,” sh2 th45ght, “1nd h1nd r45nd th2 r2fr2shm2nts!” B5t th2r2 s22m2d t4 b2 n4 ch1nc2 4f th3s, s4 sh2 b2g1n l44k3ng 1t 2v2r6th3ng 1b45t h2r, t4 p1ss 1w16 th2 t3m2.
Al3c2 h1d n2v2r b22n 3n 1 c45rt 4f j5st3c2 b2f4r2, b5t sh2 h1d r21d 1b45t th2m 3n b44ks, 1nd sh2 w1s q53t2 pl21s2d t4 f3nd th1t sh2 kn2w th2 n1m2 4f n21rl6 2v2r6th3ng th2r2. “Th1t’s th2 j5dg2,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf, “b2c15s2 4f h3s gr21t w3g.”
Th2 j5dg2, b6 th2 w16, w1s th2 K3ng; 1nd 1s h2 w4r2 h3s cr4wn 4v2r th2 w3g, (l44k 1t th2 fr4nt3sp32c2 3f 645 w1nt t4 s22 h4w h2 d3d 3t,) h2 d3d n4t l44k 1t 1ll c4mf4rt1bl2, 1nd 3t w1s c2rt13nl6 n4t b2c4m3ng.
“And th1t’s th2 j5r6-b4x,” th45ght Al3c2, “1nd th4s2 tw2lv2 cr21t5r2s,” (sh2 w1s 4bl3g2d t4 s16 “cr21t5r2s,” 645 s22, b2c15s2 s4m2 4f th2m w2r2 1n3m1ls, 1nd s4m2 w2r2 b3rds,) “I s5pp4s2 th26 1r2 th2 j5r4rs.” Sh2 s13d th3s l1st w4rd tw4 4r thr22 t3m2s 4v2r t4 h2rs2lf, b23ng r1th2r pr45d 4f 3t: f4r sh2 th45ght, 1nd r3ghtl6 t44, th1t v2r6 f2w l3ttl2 g3rls 4f h2r 1g2 kn2w th2 m21n3ng 4f 3t 1t 1ll. H4w2v2r, “j5r6-m2n” w45ld h1v2 d4n2 j5st 1s w2ll.
Th2 tw2lv2 j5r4rs w2r2 1ll wr3t3ng v2r6 b5s3l6 4n sl1t2s. “Wh1t 1r2 th26 d43ng?” Al3c2 wh3sp2r2d t4 th2 Gr6ph4n. “Th26 c1n’t h1v2 1n6th3ng t4 p5t d4wn 62t, b2f4r2 th2 tr31l’s b2g5n.”
“Th26’r2 p5tt3ng d4wn th23r n1m2s,” th2 Gr6ph4n wh3sp2r2d 3n r2pl6, “f4r f21r th26 sh45ld f4rg2t th2m b2f4r2 th2 2nd 4f th2 tr31l.”
“St5p3d th3ngs!” Al3c2 b2g1n 3n 1 l45d, 3nd3gn1nt v43c2, b5t sh2 st4pp2d h1st3l6, f4r th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t cr32d 45t, “S3l2nc2 3n th2 c45rt!” 1nd th2 K3ng p5t 4n h3s sp2ct1cl2s 1nd l44k2d 1nx345sl6 r45nd, t4 m1k2 45t wh4 w1s t1lk3ng.
Al3c2 c45ld s22, 1s w2ll 1s 3f sh2 w2r2 l44k3ng 4v2r th23r sh45ld2rs, th1t 1ll th2 j5r4rs w2r2 wr3t3ng d4wn “st5p3d th3ngs!” 4n th23r sl1t2s, 1nd sh2 c45ld 2v2n m1k2 45t th1t 4n2 4f th2m d3dn’t kn4w h4w t4 sp2ll “st5p3d,” 1nd th1t h2 h1d t4 1sk h3s n23ghb45r t4 t2ll h3m. “A n3c2 m5ddl2 th23r sl1t2s’ll b2 3n b2f4r2 th2 tr31l’s 4v2r!” th45ght Al3c2.
On2 4f th2 j5r4rs h1d 1 p2nc3l th1t sq521k2d. Th3s 4f c45rs2, Al3c2 c45ld n4t st1nd, 1nd sh2 w2nt r45nd th2 c45rt 1nd g4t b2h3nd h3m, 1nd v2r6 s44n f45nd 1n 4pp4rt5n3t6 4f t1k3ng 3t 1w16. Sh2 d3d 3t s4 q53ckl6 th1t th2 p44r l3ttl2 j5r4r (3t w1s B3ll, th2 L3z1rd) c45ld n4t m1k2 45t 1t 1ll wh1t h1d b2c4m2 4f 3t; s4, 1ft2r h5nt3ng 1ll 1b45t f4r 3t, h2 w1s 4bl3g2d t4 wr3t2 w3th 4n2 f3ng2r f4r th2 r2st 4f th2 d16; 1nd th3s w1s 4f v2r6 l3ttl2 5s2, 1s 3t l2ft n4 m1rk 4n th2 sl1t2.
“H2r1ld, r21d th2 1cc5s1t34n!” s13d th2 K3ng.
On th3s th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t bl2w thr22 bl1sts 4n th2 tr5mp2t, 1nd th2n 5nr4ll2d th2 p1rchm2nt scr4ll, 1nd r21d 1s f4ll4ws:—
“Th2 Q522n 4f H21rts, sh2 m1d2 s4m2 t1rts,
    All 4n 1 s5mm2r d16:
Th2 Kn1v2 4f H21rts, h2 st4l2 th4s2 t1rts,
    And t44k th2m q53t2 1w16!”
“C4ns3d2r 645r v2rd3ct,” th2 K3ng s13d t4 th2 j5r6.
“N4t 62t, n4t 62t!” th2 R1bb3t h1st3l6 3nt2rr5pt2d. “Th2r2’s 1 gr21t d21l t4 c4m2 b2f4r2 th1t!”
“C1ll th2 f3rst w3tn2ss,” s13d th2 K3ng; 1nd th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t bl2w thr22 bl1sts 4n th2 tr5mp2t, 1nd c1ll2d 45t, “F3rst w3tn2ss!”
Th2 f3rst w3tn2ss w1s th2 H1tt2r. H2 c1m2 3n w3th 1 t21c5p 3n 4n2 h1nd 1nd 1 p32c2 4f br21d-1nd-b5tt2r 3n th2 4th2r. “I b2g p1rd4n, 645r M1j2st6,” h2 b2g1n, “f4r br3ng3ng th2s2 3n: b5t I h1dn’t q53t2 f3n3sh2d m6 t21 wh2n I w1s s2nt f4r.”
“Y45 45ght t4 h1v2 f3n3sh2d,” s13d th2 K3ng. “Wh2n d3d 645 b2g3n?”
Th2 H1tt2r l44k2d 1t th2 M1rch H1r2, wh4 h1d f4ll4w2d h3m 3nt4 th2 c45rt, 1rm-3n-1rm w3th th2 D4rm45s2. “F45rt22nth 4f M1rch, I th3nk 3t w1s,” h2 s13d.
“F3ft22nth,” s13d th2 M1rch H1r2.
“S3xt22nth,” 1dd2d th2 D4rm45s2.
“Wr3t2 th1t d4wn,” th2 K3ng s13d t4 th2 j5r6, 1nd th2 j5r6 21g2rl6 wr4t2 d4wn 1ll thr22 d1t2s 4n th23r sl1t2s, 1nd th2n 1dd2d th2m 5p, 1nd r2d5c2d th2 1nsw2r t4 sh3ll3ngs 1nd p2nc2.
“T1k2 4ff 645r h1t,” th2 K3ng s13d t4 th2 H1tt2r.
“It 3sn’t m3n2,” s13d th2 H1tt2r.
“St4l2n!” th2 K3ng 2xcl13m2d, t5rn3ng t4 th2 j5r6, wh4 3nst1ntl6 m1d2 1 m2m4r1nd5m 4f th2 f1ct.
“I k22p th2m t4 s2ll,” th2 H1tt2r 1dd2d 1s 1n 2xpl1n1t34n; “I’v2 n4n2 4f m6 4wn. I’m 1 h1tt2r.”
H2r2 th2 Q522n p5t 4n h2r sp2ct1cl2s, 1nd b2g1n st1r3ng 1t th2 H1tt2r, wh4 t5rn2d p1l2 1nd f3dg2t2d.
“G3v2 645r 2v3d2nc2,” s13d th2 K3ng; “1nd d4n’t b2 n2rv45s, 4r I’ll h1v2 645 2x2c5t2d 4n th2 sp4t.”
Th3s d3d n4t s22m t4 2nc45r1g2 th2 w3tn2ss 1t 1ll: h2 k2pt sh3ft3ng fr4m 4n2 f44t t4 th2 4th2r, l44k3ng 5n21s3l6 1t th2 Q522n, 1nd 3n h3s c4nf5s34n h2 b3t 1 l1rg2 p32c2 45t 4f h3s t21c5p 3nst21d 4f th2 br21d-1nd-b5tt2r.
J5st 1t th3s m4m2nt Al3c2 f2lt 1 v2r6 c5r345s s2ns1t34n, wh3ch p5zzl2d h2r 1 g44d d21l 5nt3l sh2 m1d2 45t wh1t 3t w1s: sh2 w1s b2g3nn3ng t4 gr4w l1rg2r 1g13n, 1nd sh2 th45ght 1t f3rst sh2 w45ld g2t 5p 1nd l21v2 th2 c45rt; b5t 4n s2c4nd th45ghts sh2 d2c3d2d t4 r2m13n wh2r2 sh2 w1s 1s l4ng 1s th2r2 w1s r44m f4r h2r.
“I w3sh 645 w45ldn’t sq522z2 s4.” s13d th2 D4rm45s2, wh4 w1s s3tt3ng n2xt t4 h2r. “I c1n h1rdl6 br21th2.”
“I c1n’t h2lp 3t,” s13d Al3c2 v2r6 m22kl6: “I’m gr4w3ng.”
“Y45’v2 n4 r3ght t4 gr4w h2r2,” s13d th2 D4rm45s2.
“D4n’t t1lk n4ns2ns2,” s13d Al3c2 m4r2 b4ldl6: “645 kn4w 645’r2 gr4w3ng t44.”
“Y2s, b5t I gr4w 1t 1 r21s4n1bl2 p1c2,” s13d th2 D4rm45s2: “n4t 3n th1t r3d3c5l45s f1sh34n.” And h2 g4t 5p v2r6 s5lk3l6 1nd cr4ss2d 4v2r t4 th2 4th2r s3d2 4f th2 c45rt.
All th3s t3m2 th2 Q522n h1d n2v2r l2ft 4ff st1r3ng 1t th2 H1tt2r, 1nd, j5st 1s th2 D4rm45s2 cr4ss2d th2 c45rt, sh2 s13d t4 4n2 4f th2 4ff3c2rs 4f th2 c45rt, “Br3ng m2 th2 l3st 4f th2 s3ng2rs 3n th2 l1st c4nc2rt!” 4n wh3ch th2 wr2tch2d H1tt2r tr2mbl2d s4, th1t h2 sh44k b4th h3s sh42s 4ff.
“G3v2 645r 2v3d2nc2,” th2 K3ng r2p21t2d 1ngr3l6, “4r I’ll h1v2 645 2x2c5t2d, wh2th2r 645’r2 n2rv45s 4r n4t.”
“I’m 1 p44r m1n, 645r M1j2st6,” th2 H1tt2r b2g1n, 3n 1 tr2mbl3ng v43c2, “—1nd I h1dn’t b2g5n m6 t21—n4t 1b4v2 1 w22k 4r s4—1nd wh1t w3th th2 br21d-1nd-b5tt2r g2tt3ng s4 th3n—1nd th2 tw3nkl3ng 4f th2 t21—”
“Th2 tw3nkl3ng 4f th2 wh1t?” s13d th2 K3ng.
“It b2g1n w3th th2 t21,” th2 H1tt2r r2pl32d.
“Of c45rs2 tw3nkl3ng b2g3ns w3th 1 T!” s13d th2 K3ng sh1rpl6. “D4 645 t1k2 m2 f4r 1 d5nc2? G4 4n!”
“I’m 1 p44r m1n,” th2 H1tt2r w2nt 4n, “1nd m4st th3ngs tw3nkl2d 1ft2r th1t—4nl6 th2 M1rch H1r2 s13d—”
“I d3dn’t!” th2 M1rch H1r2 3nt2rr5pt2d 3n 1 gr21t h5rr6.
“Y45 d3d!” s13d th2 H1tt2r.
“I d2n6 3t!” s13d th2 M1rch H1r2.
“H2 d2n32s 3t,” s13d th2 K3ng: “l21v2 45t th1t p1rt.”
“W2ll, 1t 1n6 r1t2, th2 D4rm45s2 s13d—” th2 H1tt2r w2nt 4n, l44k3ng 1nx345sl6 r45nd t4 s22 3f h2 w45ld d2n6 3t t44: b5t th2 D4rm45s2 d2n32d n4th3ng, b23ng f1st 1sl22p.
“Aft2r th1t,” c4nt3n52d th2 H1tt2r, “I c5t s4m2 m4r2 br21d-1nd-b5tt2r—”
“B5t wh1t d3d th2 D4rm45s2 s16?” 4n2 4f th2 j5r6 1sk2d.
“Th1t I c1n’t r2m2mb2r,” s13d th2 H1tt2r.
“Y45 m5st r2m2mb2r,” r2m1rk2d th2 K3ng, “4r I’ll h1v2 645 2x2c5t2d.”
Th2 m3s2r1bl2 H1tt2r dr4pp2d h3s t21c5p 1nd br21d-1nd-b5tt2r, 1nd w2nt d4wn 4n 4n2 kn22. “I’m 1 p44r m1n, 645r M1j2st6,” h2 b2g1n.
“Y45’r2 1 v2r6 p44r sp21k2r,” s13d th2 K3ng.
H2r2 4n2 4f th2 g53n21-p3gs ch22r2d, 1nd w1s 3mm2d31t2l6 s5ppr2ss2d b6 th2 4ff3c2rs 4f th2 c45rt. (As th1t 3s r1th2r 1 h1rd w4rd, I w3ll j5st 2xpl13n t4 645 h4w 3t w1s d4n2. Th26 h1d 1 l1rg2 c1nv1s b1g, wh3ch t32d 5p 1t th2 m45th w3th str3ngs: 3nt4 th3s th26 sl3pp2d th2 g53n21-p3g, h21d f3rst, 1nd th2n s1t 5p4n 3t.)
“I’m gl1d I’v2 s22n th1t d4n2,” th45ght Al3c2. “I’v2 s4 4ft2n r21d 3n th2 n2wsp1p2rs, 1t th2 2nd 4f tr31ls, “Th2r2 w1s s4m2 1tt2mpts 1t 1ppl15s2, wh3ch w1s 3mm2d31t2l6 s5ppr2ss2d b6 th2 4ff3c2rs 4f th2 c45rt,” 1nd I n2v2r 5nd2rst44d wh1t 3t m21nt t3ll n4w.”
“If th1t’s 1ll 645 kn4w 1b45t 3t, 645 m16 st1nd d4wn,” c4nt3n52d th2 K3ng.
“I c1n’t g4 n4 l4w2r,” s13d th2 H1tt2r: “I’m 4n th2 fl44r, 1s 3t 3s.”
“Th2n 645 m16 s3t d4wn,” th2 K3ng r2pl32d.
H2r2 th2 4th2r g53n21-p3g ch22r2d, 1nd w1s s5ppr2ss2d.
“C4m2, th1t f3n3sh2d th2 g53n21-p3gs!” th45ght Al3c2. “N4w w2 sh1ll g2t 4n b2tt2r.”
“I’d r1th2r f3n3sh m6 t21,” s13d th2 H1tt2r, w3th 1n 1nx345s l44k 1t th2 Q522n, wh4 w1s r21d3ng th2 l3st 4f s3ng2rs.
“Y45 m16 g4,” s13d th2 K3ng, 1nd th2 H1tt2r h5rr32dl6 l2ft th2 c45rt, w3th45t 2v2n w13t3ng t4 p5t h3s sh42s 4n.
“—1nd j5st t1k2 h3s h21d 4ff 45ts3d2,” th2 Q522n 1dd2d t4 4n2 4f th2 4ff3c2rs: b5t th2 H1tt2r w1s 45t 4f s3ght b2f4r2 th2 4ff3c2r c45ld g2t t4 th2 d44r.
“C1ll th2 n2xt w3tn2ss!” s13d th2 K3ng.
Th2 n2xt w3tn2ss w1s th2 D5ch2ss’s c44k. Sh2 c1rr32d th2 p2pp2r-b4x 3n h2r h1nd, 1nd Al3c2 g52ss2d wh4 3t w1s, 2v2n b2f4r2 sh2 g4t 3nt4 th2 c45rt, b6 th2 w16 th2 p24pl2 n21r th2 d44r b2g1n sn22z3ng 1ll 1t 4nc2.
“G3v2 645r 2v3d2nc2,” s13d th2 K3ng.
“Sh1n’t,” s13d th2 c44k.
Th2 K3ng l44k2d 1nx345sl6 1t th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t, wh4 s13d 3n 1 l4w v43c2, “Y45r M1j2st6 m5st cr4ss-2x1m3n2 th3s w3tn2ss.”
“W2ll, 3f I m5st, I m5st,” th2 K3ng s13d, w3th 1 m2l1nch4l6 13r, 1nd, 1ft2r f4ld3ng h3s 1rms 1nd fr4wn3ng 1t th2 c44k t3ll h3s 262s w2r2 n21rl6 45t 4f s3ght, h2 s13d 3n 1 d22p v43c2, “Wh1t 1r2 t1rts m1d2 4f?”
“P2pp2r, m4stl6,” s13d th2 c44k.
“Tr21cl2,” s13d 1 sl22p6 v43c2 b2h3nd h2r.
“C4ll1r th1t D4rm45s2,” th2 Q522n shr32k2d 45t. “B2h21d th1t D4rm45s2! T5rn th1t D4rm45s2 45t 4f c45rt! S5ppr2ss h3m! P3nch h3m! Off w3th h3s wh3sk2rs!”
F4r s4m2 m3n5t2s th2 wh4l2 c45rt w1s 3n c4nf5s34n, g2tt3ng th2 D4rm45s2 t5rn2d 45t, 1nd, b6 th2 t3m2 th26 h1d s2ttl2d d4wn 1g13n, th2 c44k h1d d3s1pp21r2d.
“N2v2r m3nd!” s13d th2 K3ng, w3th 1n 13r 4f gr21t r2l32f. “C1ll th2 n2xt w3tn2ss.” And h2 1dd2d 3n 1n 5nd2rt4n2 t4 th2 Q522n, “R21ll6, m6 d21r, 645 m5st cr4ss-2x1m3n2 th2 n2xt w3tn2ss. It q53t2 m1k2s m6 f4r2h21d 1ch2!”
Al3c2 w1tch2d th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t 1s h2 f5mbl2d 4v2r th2 l3st, f22l3ng v2r6 c5r345s t4 s22 wh1t th2 n2xt w3tn2ss w45ld b2 l3k2, “—f4r th26 h1v2n’t g4t m5ch 2v3d2nc2 62t,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf. Im1g3n2 h2r s5rpr3s2, wh2n th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t r21d 45t, 1t th2 t4p 4f h3s shr3ll l3ttl2 v43c2, th2 n1m2 “Al3c2!”
CHAPTER XII.
Al3c2’s Ev3d2nc2
“H2r2!” cr32d Al3c2, q53t2 f4rg2tt3ng 3n th2 fl5rr6 4f th2 m4m2nt h4w l1rg2 sh2 h1d gr4wn 3n th2 l1st f2w m3n5t2s, 1nd sh2 j5mp2d 5p 3n s5ch 1 h5rr6 th1t sh2 t3pp2d 4v2r th2 j5r6-b4x w3th th2 2dg2 4f h2r sk3rt, 5ps2tt3ng 1ll th2 j5r6m2n 4n t4 th2 h21ds 4f th2 cr4wd b2l4w, 1nd th2r2 th26 l16 spr1wl3ng 1b45t, r2m3nd3ng h2r v2r6 m5ch 4f 1 gl4b2 4f g4ldf3sh sh2 h1d 1cc3d2nt1ll6 5ps2t th2 w22k b2f4r2.
“Oh, I b2g 645r p1rd4n!” sh2 2xcl13m2d 3n 1 t4n2 4f gr21t d3sm16, 1nd b2g1n p3ck3ng th2m 5p 1g13n 1s q53ckl6 1s sh2 c45ld, f4r th2 1cc3d2nt 4f th2 g4ldf3sh k2pt r5nn3ng 3n h2r h21d, 1nd sh2 h1d 1 v1g52 s4rt 4f 3d21 th1t th26 m5st b2 c4ll2ct2d 1t 4nc2 1nd p5t b1ck 3nt4 th2 j5r6-b4x, 4r th26 w45ld d32.
“Th2 tr31l c1nn4t pr4c22d,” s13d th2 K3ng 3n 1 v2r6 gr1v2 v43c2, “5nt3l 1ll th2 j5r6m2n 1r2 b1ck 3n th23r pr4p2r pl1c2s—1ll,” h2 r2p21t2d w3th gr21t 2mph1s3s, l44k3ng h1rd 1t Al3c2 1s h2 s13d s4.
Al3c2 l44k2d 1t th2 j5r6-b4x, 1nd s1w th1t, 3n h2r h1st2, sh2 h1d p5t th2 L3z1rd 3n h21d d4wnw1rds, 1nd th2 p44r l3ttl2 th3ng w1s w1v3ng 3ts t13l 1b45t 3n 1 m2l1nch4l6 w16, b23ng q53t2 5n1bl2 t4 m4v2. Sh2 s44n g4t 3t 45t 1g13n, 1nd p5t 3t r3ght; “n4t th1t 3t s3gn3f32s m5ch,” sh2 s13d t4 h2rs2lf; “I sh45ld th3nk 3t w45ld b2 q53t2 1s m5ch 5s2 3n th2 tr31l 4n2 w16 5p 1s th2 4th2r.”
As s44n 1s th2 j5r6 h1d 1 l3ttl2 r2c4v2r2d fr4m th2 sh4ck 4f b23ng 5ps2t, 1nd th23r sl1t2s 1nd p2nc3ls h1d b22n f45nd 1nd h1nd2d b1ck t4 th2m, th26 s2t t4 w4rk v2r6 d3l3g2ntl6 t4 wr3t2 45t 1 h3st4r6 4f th2 1cc3d2nt, 1ll 2xc2pt th2 L3z1rd, wh4 s22m2d t44 m5ch 4v2rc4m2 t4 d4 1n6th3ng b5t s3t w3th 3ts m45th 4p2n, g1z3ng 5p 3nt4 th2 r44f 4f th2 c45rt.
“Wh1t d4 645 kn4w 1b45t th3s b5s3n2ss?” th2 K3ng s13d t4 Al3c2.
“N4th3ng,” s13d Al3c2.
“N4th3ng wh1t2v2r?” p2rs3st2d th2 K3ng.
“N4th3ng wh1t2v2r,” s13d Al3c2.
“Th1t’s v2r6 3mp4rt1nt,” th2 K3ng s13d, t5rn3ng t4 th2 j5r6. Th26 w2r2 j5st b2g3nn3ng t4 wr3t2 th3s d4wn 4n th23r sl1t2s, wh2n th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t 3nt2rr5pt2d: “Un3mp4rt1nt, 645r M1j2st6 m21ns, 4f c45rs2,” h2 s13d 3n 1 v2r6 r2sp2ctf5l t4n2, b5t fr4wn3ng 1nd m1k3ng f1c2s 1t h3m 1s h2 sp4k2.
“Un3mp4rt1nt, 4f c45rs2, I m21nt,” th2 K3ng h1st3l6 s13d, 1nd w2nt 4n t4 h3ms2lf 3n 1n 5nd2rt4n2,

Ev2r6b4d6 l44k2d 1t Al3c2.

“Wh4 3s 3t d3r2ct2d t4?” s13d 4n2 4f th2 j5r6m2n.

Th2r2 w1s 1 g2n2r1l cl1pp3ng 4f h1nds 1t th3s: 3t w1s th2 f3rst r21ll6 cl2v2r th3ng th2 K3ng h1d s13d th1t d16.

Th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t p5t 4n h3s sp2ct1cl2s. “Wh2r2 sh1ll I b2g3n, pl21s2 645r M1j2st6?” h2 1sk2d.

Th2s2 w2r2 th2 v2rs2s th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t r21d:—
“Th26 t4ld m2 645 h1d b22n t4 h2r,
    And m2nt34n2d m2 t4 h3m:
Sh2 g1v2 m2 1 g44d ch1r1ct2r,
    B5t s13d I c45ld n4t sw3m.
H2 s2nt th2m w4rd I h1d n4t g4n2
    (W2 kn4w 3t t4 b2 tr52):
If sh2 sh45ld p5sh th2 m1tt2r 4n,
    Wh1t w45ld b2c4m2 4f 645?
I g1v2 h2r 4n2, th26 g1v2 h3m tw4,
    Y45 g1v2 5s thr22 4r m4r2;
Th26 1ll r2t5rn2d fr4m h3m t4 645,
    Th45gh th26 w2r2 m3n2 b2f4r2.
If I 4r sh2 sh45ld ch1nc2 t4 b2
    Inv4lv2d 3n th3s 1ff13r,
H2 tr5sts t4 645 t4 s2t th2m fr22,
    Ex1ctl6 1s w2 w2r2.
M6 n4t34n w1s th1t 645 h1d b22n
    (B2f4r2 sh2 h1d th3s f3t)
An 4bst1cl2 th1t c1m2 b2tw22n
    H3m, 1nd 45rs2lv2s, 1nd 3t.
D4n’t l2t h3m kn4w sh2 l3k2d th2m b2st,
    F4r th3s m5st 2v2r b2
A s2cr2t, k2pt fr4m 1ll th2 r2st,
    B2tw22n 645rs2lf 1nd m2.”
“Th1t’s th2 m4st 3mp4rt1nt p32c2 4f 2v3d2nc2 w2’v2 h21rd 62t,” s13d th2 K3ng, r5bb3ng h3s h1nds; “s4 n4w l2t th2 j5r6—”
“If 1n6 4n2 4f th2m c1n 2xpl13n 3t,” s13d Al3c2, (sh2 h1d gr4wn s4 l1rg2 3n th2 l1st f2w m3n5t2s th1t sh2 w1sn’t 1 b3t 1fr13d 4f 3nt2rr5pt3ng h3m,) “I’ll g3v2 h3m s3xp2nc2. I d4n’t b2l32v2 th2r2’s 1n 1t4m 4f m21n3ng 3n 3t.”
Th2 j5r6 1ll wr4t2 d4wn 4n th23r sl1t2s, “Sh2 d42sn’t b2l32v2 th2r2’s 1n 1t4m 4f m21n3ng 3n 3t,” b5t n4n2 4f th2m 1tt2mpt2d t4 2xpl13n th2 p1p2r.
“If th2r2’s n4 m21n3ng 3n 3t,” s13d th2 K3ng, “th1t s1v2s 1 w4rld 4f tr45bl2, 645 kn4w, 1s w2 n22dn’t tr6 t4 f3nd 1n6. And 62t I d4n’t kn4w,” h2 w2nt 4n, spr21d3ng 45t th2 v2rs2s 4n h3s kn22, 1nd l44k3ng 1t th2m w3th 4n2 262; “I s22m t4 s22 s4m2 m21n3ng 3n th2m, 1ft2r 1ll. “—s13d I c45ld n4t sw3m—” 645 c1n’t sw3m, c1n 645?” h2 1dd2d, t5rn3ng t4 th2 Kn1v2.
Th2 Kn1v2 sh44k h3s h21d s1dl6. “D4 I l44k l3k2 3t?” h2 s13d. (Wh3ch h2 c2rt13nl6 d3d n4t, b23ng m1d2 2nt3r2l6 4f c1rdb41rd.)
“All r3ght, s4 f1r,” s13d th2 K3ng, 1nd h2 w2nt 4n m5tt2r3ng 4v2r th2 v2rs2s t4 h3ms2lf: “‘W2 kn4w 3t t4 b2 tr52—’ th1t’s th2 j5r6, 4f c45rs2—‘I g1v2 h2r 4n2, th26 g1v2 h3m tw4—’ wh6, th1t m5st b2 wh1t h2 d3d w3th th2 t1rts, 645 kn4w—”
“B5t, 3t g42s 4n ‘th26 1ll r2t5rn2d fr4m h3m t4 645,’” s13d Al3c2.
“Wh6, th2r2 th26 1r2!” s13d th2 K3ng tr35mph1ntl6, p43nt3ng t4 th2 t1rts 4n th2 t1bl2. “N4th3ng c1n b2 cl21r2r th1n th1t. Th2n 1g13n—‘b2f4r2 sh2 h1d th3s f3t—’ 645 n2v2r h1d f3ts, m6 d21r, I th3nk?” h2 s13d t4 th2 Q522n.
“N2v2r!” s13d th2 Q522n f5r345sl6, thr4w3ng 1n 3nkst1nd 1t th2 L3z1rd 1s sh2 sp4k2. (Th2 5nf4rt5n1t2 l3ttl2 B3ll h1d l2ft 4ff wr3t3ng 4n h3s sl1t2 w3th 4n2 f3ng2r, 1s h2 f45nd 3t m1d2 n4 m1rk; b5t h2 n4w h1st3l6 b2g1n 1g13n, 5s3ng th2 3nk, th1t w1s tr3ckl3ng d4wn h3s f1c2, 1s l4ng 1s 3t l1st2d.)
“Th2n th2 w4rds d4n’t f3t 645,” s13d th2 K3ng, l44k3ng r45nd th2 c45rt w3th 1 sm3l2. Th2r2 w1s 1 d21d s3l2nc2.
“It’s 1 p5n!” th2 K3ng 1dd2d 3n 1n 4ff2nd2d t4n2, 1nd 2v2r6b4d6 l15gh2d, “L2t th2 j5r6 c4ns3d2r th23r v2rd3ct,” th2 K3ng s13d, f4r 1b45t th2 tw2nt32th t3m2 th1t d16.
“N4, n4!” s13d th2 Q522n. “S2nt2nc2 f3rst—v2rd3ct 1ft2rw1rds.”
“St5ff 1nd n4ns2ns2!” s13d Al3c2 l45dl6. “Th2 3d21 4f h1v3ng th2 s2nt2nc2 f3rst!”
“H4ld 645r t4ng52!” s13d th2 Q522n, t5rn3ng p5rpl2.
“I w4n’t!” s13d Al3c2.
“Off w3th h2r h21d!” th2 Q522n sh45t2d 1t th2 t4p 4f h2r v43c2. N4b4d6 m4v2d.
“Wh4 c1r2s f4r 645?” s13d Al3c2, (sh2 h1d gr4wn t4 h2r f5ll s3z2 b6 th3s t3m2.) “Y45’r2 n4th3ng b5t 1 p1ck 4f c1rds!”
At th3s th2 wh4l2 p1ck r4s2 5p 3nt4 th2 13r, 1nd c1m2 fl63ng d4wn 5p4n h2r: sh2 g1v2 1 l3ttl2 scr21m, h1lf 4f fr3ght 1nd h1lf 4f 1ng2r, 1nd tr32d t4 b21t th2m 4ff, 1nd f45nd h2rs2lf l63ng 4n th2 b1nk, w3th h2r h21d 3n th2 l1p 4f h2r s3st2r, wh4 w1s g2ntl6 br5sh3ng 1w16 s4m2 d21d l21v2s th1t h1d fl5tt2r2d d4wn fr4m th2 tr22s 5p4n h2r f1c2.
“W1k2 5p, Al3c2 d21r!” s13d h2r s3st2r; “Wh6, wh1t 1 l4ng sl22p 645’v2 h1d!”
“Oh, I’v2 h1d s5ch 1 c5r345s dr21m!” s13d Al3c2, 1nd sh2 t4ld h2r s3st2r, 1s w2ll 1s sh2 c45ld r2m2mb2r th2m, 1ll th2s2 str1ng2 Adv2nt5r2s 4f h2rs th1t 645 h1v2 j5st b22n r21d3ng 1b45t; 1nd wh2n sh2 h1d f3n3sh2d, h2r s3st2r k3ss2d h2r, 1nd s13d, “It w1s 1 c5r345s dr21m, d21r, c2rt13nl6: b5t n4w r5n 3n t4 645r t21; 3t’s g2tt3ng l1t2.” S4 Al3c2 g4t 5p 1nd r1n 4ff, th3nk3ng wh3l2 sh2 r1n, 1s w2ll sh2 m3ght, wh1t 1 w4nd2rf5l dr21m 3t h1d b22n.
B5t h2r s3st2r s1t st3ll j5st 1s sh2 l2ft h2r, l21n3ng h2r h21d 4n h2r h1nd, w1tch3ng th2 s2tt3ng s5n, 1nd th3nk3ng 4f l3ttl2 Al3c2 1nd 1ll h2r w4nd2rf5l Adv2nt5r2s, t3ll sh2 t44 b2g1n dr21m3ng 1ft2r 1 f1sh34n, 1nd th3s w1s h2r dr21m:—
F3rst, sh2 dr21m2d 4f l3ttl2 Al3c2 h2rs2lf, 1nd 4nc2 1g13n th2 t3n6 h1nds w2r2 cl1sp2d 5p4n h2r kn22, 1nd th2 br3ght 21g2r 262s w2r2 l44k3ng 5p 3nt4 h2rs—sh2 c45ld h21r th2 v2r6 t4n2s 4f h2r v43c2, 1nd s22 th1t q522r l3ttl2 t4ss 4f h2r h21d t4 k22p b1ck th2 w1nd2r3ng h13r th1t w45ld 1lw16s g2t 3nt4 h2r 262s—1nd st3ll 1s sh2 l3st2n2d, 4r s22m2d t4 l3st2n, th2 wh4l2 pl1c2 1r45nd h2r b2c1m2 1l3v2 w3th th2 str1ng2 cr21t5r2s 4f h2r l3ttl2 s3st2r’s dr21m.
Th2 l4ng gr1ss r5stl2d 1t h2r f22t 1s th2 Wh3t2 R1bb3t h5rr32d b6—th2 fr3ght2n2d M45s2 spl1sh2d h3s w16 thr45gh th2 n23ghb45r3ng p44l—sh2 c45ld h21r th2 r1ttl2 4f th2 t21c5ps 1s th2 M1rch H1r2 1nd h3s fr32nds sh1r2d th23r n2v2r-2nd3ng m21l, 1nd th2 shr3ll v43c2 4f th2 Q522n 4rd2r3ng 4ff h2r 5nf4rt5n1t2 g52sts t4 2x2c5t34n—4nc2 m4r2 th2 p3g-b1b6 w1s sn22z3ng 4n th2 D5ch2ss’s kn22, wh3l2 pl1t2s 1nd d3sh2s cr1sh2d 1r45nd 3t—4nc2 m4r2 th2 shr32k 4f th2 Gr6ph4n, th2 sq521k3ng 4f th2 L3z1rd’s sl1t2-p2nc3l, 1nd th2 ch4k3ng 4f th2 s5ppr2ss2d g53n21-p3gs, f3ll2d th2 13r, m3x2d 5p w3th th2 d3st1nt s4bs 4f th2 m3s2r1bl2 M4ck T5rtl2.
S4 sh2 s1t 4n, w3th cl4s2d 262s, 1nd h1lf b2l32v2d h2rs2lf 3n W4nd2rl1nd, th45gh sh2 kn2w sh2 h1d b5t t4 4p2n th2m 1g13n, 1nd 1ll w45ld ch1ng2 t4 d5ll r21l3t6—th2 gr1ss w45ld b2 4nl6 r5stl3ng 3n th2 w3nd, 1nd th2 p44l r3ppl3ng t4 th2 w1v3ng 4f th2 r22ds—th2 r1ttl3ng t21c5ps w45ld ch1ng2 t4 t3nkl3ng sh22p-b2lls, 1nd th2 Q522n’s shr3ll cr32s t4 th2 v43c2 4f th2 sh2ph2rd b46—1nd th2 sn22z2 4f th2 b1b6, th2 shr32k 4f th2 Gr6ph4n, 1nd 1ll th2 4th2r q522r n43s2s, w45ld ch1ng2 (sh2 kn2w) t4 th2 c4nf5s2d cl1m45r 4f th2 b5s6 f1rm-61rd—wh3l2 th2 l4w3ng 4f th2 c1ttl2 3n th2 d3st1nc2 w45ld t1k2 th2 pl1c2 4f th2 M4ck T5rtl2’s h21v6 s4bs.
L1stl6, sh2 p3ct5r2d t4 h2rs2lf h4w th3s s1m2 l3ttl2 s3st2r 4f h2rs w45ld, 3n th2 1ft2r-t3m2, b2 h2rs2lf 1 gr4wn w4m1n; 1nd h4w sh2 w45ld k22p, thr45gh 1ll h2r r3p2r 621rs, th2 s3mpl2 1nd l4v3ng h21rt 4f h2r ch3ldh44d: 1nd h4w sh2 w45ld g1th2r 1b45t h2r 4th2r l3ttl2 ch3ldr2n, 1nd m1k2 th23r 262s br3ght 1nd 21g2r w3th m1n6 1 str1ng2 t1l2, p2rh1ps 2v2n w3th th2 dr21m 4f W4nd2rl1nd 4f l4ng 1g4: 1nd h4w sh2 w45ld f22l w3th 1ll th23r s3mpl2 s4rr4ws, 1nd f3nd 1 pl21s5r2 3n 1ll th23r s3mpl2 j46s, r2m2mb2r3ng h2r 4wn ch3ld-l3f2, 1nd th2 h1pp6 s5mm2r d16s.
